Now I have the complete picture. Here is my analysis:

---

## Root Cause Analysis: `scanAll` reports 0 files for assets directories

### The Bug: Path format mismatch

The stored config value for an asset directory (as returned by `asset-picker.svelte`'s `getRelPath()`) is `assets/<folder_name>` — note: **no `/data/` prefix**.

| Code path | Path passed to `readDir` API | Result |
|-----------|------------------------------|--------|
| **`sources-tab.svelte` `refreshAll()`** (lines 57-61) | `/data/assets/<folder>/` | ✅ Works |
| **`sourceManager.ts` `scanAll()`** (line 22) | `assets/<folder>` (raw config value) | ❌ Fails |

### Why it fails

`scanAll` passes the raw config value directly to `scanSource`:

```typescript
// sourceManager.ts:22 — NO normalization
const items = await scanSource('assets', dir)  // dir = "assets/bg"
```

This flows into `readDir()` in `api.ts`, which calls:
```
POST /api/file/readDir { path: "assets/bg" }
```

The SiYuan kernel's `/api/file/readDir` API requires paths relative to the workspace root. An assets folder physically lives at `data/assets/bg/` in the workspace. The API does **not** find `assets/bg` as a valid path, so it returns an error (`code != 0`). In `readDir()` (line 22), the `!Array.isArray(data)` guard catches the error and silently returns `[]`. No exception is thrown.

Meanwhile, `sources-tab.svelte` `refreshAll()` (lines 57-61) normalizes the same config value **before** the API call:

```typescript
// sources-tab.svelte:57-61 — NORMALIZES the path
const normalized = dir.startsWith('/data/assets/') ? `assets/${dir.slice('/data/assets/'.length)}`
    : dir.startsWith('data/assets/') ? `assets/${dir.slice('data/assets/'.length)}`
    : dir
const path = `/data/${normalized}`            // → "/data/assets/bg"
const files = await scanSource('assets', path + '/')  // → "/data/assets/bg/"
```

This produces `/data/assets/bg/`, which the kernel API correctly resolves.

### Impact

All callers of `scanAll` are affected:

| Caller (in `index.ts`) | Trigger | Consequence |
|------------------------|---------|-------------|
| `onload()` line 77 | Plugin startup, when `currentFile` is null | Pool is empty → falls back to default background |
| `randomSelect()` line 140 | `⇧⌘F7` hotkey / topbar "随机抽一张" | Pool is empty → "pool is empty, nothing to pick" |

But opening the Settings UI → Sources tab works fine because it calls `refreshAll()`, which does normalize.

### Where the fix belongs

The normalization should be added in **`scanAll` (or `scanSource`)** — either way makes it consistent. The ideal fix matches the normalization logic that already exists in `sources-tab.svelte:57-61`:

```typescript
// In sourceManager.ts, before calling scanSource for asset type dirs:
for (const dir of assetDirs) {
    if (dir.length === 0) continue
    const normalized = dir.startsWith('/data/assets/') ? `assets/${dir.slice('/data/assets/'.length)}`
        : dir.startsWith('data/assets/') ? `assets/${dir.slice('data/assets/'.length)}`
        : dir
    const path = `/data/${normalized}`
    const items = await scanSource('assets', path + '/')
    ...
}
```

> **Note:** The `getFileUrl()` in `fs.ts` handles both `/data/`-prefixed and unprefixed paths correctly (strips the prefix for canvas CSS), so normalizing the path for the `readDir` API call won't break URL construction.

Nya~♡
</task_result>
```

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

The subagent has identified the root cause. Let me verify this by reading the actual source code to confirm the findings.

The issue is:
1. `asset-picker.svelte` stores asset directory paths as `assets/<folder_name>` (without `/data/` prefix)
2. `sources-tab.svelte` normalizes this path before calling `scanSource` by prepending `/data/`
3. `sourceManager.ts` `scanAll()` does NOT normalize the path, passing raw `assets/<folder>` to the API
4. The kernel API needs the full workspace path, so it fails and returns 0 files
5. `randomSelect()` uses `scanAll()` → pool is empty → "pool is empty, nothing to pick"

The fix should be in `sourceManager.ts` to normalize the path. Let me read the actual files to confirm the exact code and prepare the fix.

82:     }

85: }

87: export function pickRandom(items: ImageItem[], excludeUrl?: string | null): ImageItem | null {
88:     if (items.length === 0) return null
89: 
90:     if (excludeUrl) {
91:         const filtered = items.filter(item => item.url !== excludeUrl)
92:         if (filtered.length === 0) return null
93:         const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * filtered.length)
94:         return filtered[idx]
95:     }
96: 
97:     const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * items.length)
98:     return items[idx]
99: }

102:     if (path.length === 0) return false
103: 
104:     if (isDesktop()) {

106:             await (window as any).require('fs/promises').access(path)
107:             return true
108:         } catch {
109:             return false
110:         }
111:     }
112: 
113:     try {
114:         await readDirKernel(path)
115:         return true
116:     } catch {
117:         return false
118:     }
119: }

216:                 }

221:     async function clearCache() {
222:         const group = groups.find(g => g.type === 'upload')
223:         if (!group || group.files.length === 0) return

228:         if (vidCount > 0) parts.push(`${vidCount} ${i18n.videoCount ?? 'videos'}`)

263:                 }

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

Now I can confirm the root cause. Let me also check how the asset directory is stored in the config to understand what path format it uses.

The user's HTML shows `assets/title/subfolder2` as the display label in the sources tab. The log shows:
```
[bgCover] sourceManager scanAll assets[assets/title/subfolder2]: 0 个文件
```

And in sources-tab.svelte line 57-61:
```typescript
const normalized = dir.startsWith('/data/assets/') ? `assets/${dir.slice('/data/assets/'.length)}`
    : dir.startsWith('data/assets/') ? `assets/${dir.slice('data/assets/'.length)}`
    : dir
const path = `/data/${normalized}`
```

So `sources-tab.svelte` takes the stored config value (which is something like `assets/title/subfolder2`), normalizes it, and prepends `/data/` to get `/data/assets/title/subfolder2`.

But in `sourceManager.ts` line 22:
```typescript
const items = await scanSource('assets', dir)
```

It passes the raw config value `assets/title/subfolder2` directly to `readDirKernel()`, which sends a request to `/api/file/readDir` with `{ path: "assets/title/subfolder2" }`. The kernel API doesn't recognize this path, so it fails and returns `[]`.

The fix is straightforward: add the same path normalization logic in `sourceManager.ts`'s `scanAll` function, just like what `sources-tab.svelte` does in `refreshAll()`.

Let me formulate the plan:

1. In `sourceManager.ts`, in the `scanAll` function, normalize the `dir` for asset sources by prepending `/data/` to it (similar to what `sources-tab.svelte` does at lines 57-62).
2. The normalization logic should handle:
   - Paths already prefixed with `/data/assets/`
   - Paths already prefixed with `data/assets/`
   - Paths like `assets/folder` (no `/data/` prefix) — common case from asset-picker
3. The fix should also pass the path with a trailing `/` for consistency (like `sources-tab.svelte` does).

Let me also verify the `getFileUrl` logic in `fs.ts` to make sure that the normalized path (with `/data/` prefix) won't break URL construction.

Let me read `fs.ts` for the `getFileUrl` function.

</details>

| **26** | `src/utils/fs.ts` | 35-44 | `getFileUrl(apiPath, 'assets')` | Handles all input formats → `assets/subfolder/img.jpg` | Canvas URL construction | ✅ Robust |

| **29** | `tests/stores/config.test.ts` | 60 | `assetDirs: []` | `assets/subfolder` format | Test default | ✅ |

---

### Issues Found

#### ⚠️ Issue A — `scanAll` passes `assets/subfolder` (relative) to kernel API instead of `/data/assets/subfolder` (absolute)

- **Location**: `src/services/sourceManager.ts` lines 20-22, `src/index.ts` lines 75-77 and 138-140
- **What happens**: `scanAll` reads `assetDirs` entries like `['assets/subfolder']` and passes them directly to `scanSource('assets', 'assets/subfolder')`. This in turn calls `readDirKernel('assets/subfolder')` → `readDir('assets/subfolder')` → `fetchSyncPost('/api/file/readDir', { path: 'assets/subfolder' })`.
- **Contrast**: `sources-tab.svelte` line 60-62 does the same path normalization differently: it converts to `/data/assets/subfolder/` first.
- **Impact**: The siyuan kernel resolves `/api/file/readDir` paths relative to the workspace root. `assets/` under the workspace root resolves to `{workspace}/data/assets/` — this *may* work (siyuan uses a `data` directory). But it depends on kernel behavior and is inconsistent with how the same code path constructs paths in `sources-tab.svelte`.
- **Recommended fix**: Have `scanAll` normalize asset dirs the same way — prepend `/data/`:
  ```ts
  // In scanAll, before scanSource call:
  const normalized = dir.startsWith('/data/') ? dir : `/data/${dir}`
  const items = await scanSource('assets', normalized)
  ```

#### ⚠️ Issue B — Two different normalization logics exist (duplicated, slightly different)

- **Location 1**: `src/ui/sources/asset-picker.svelte` lines 115-118 (`getRelPath`)
- **Location 2**: `src/ui/settings/sources-tab.svelte` lines 57-59 (inline normalization)
- **Location 3**: `src/services/sourceManager.ts` line 126 (`getSourceLabel` — checks only `data/assets/` without leading `/`)
- **What happens**: The same "strip data prefix, return assets-prefixed path" logic is duplicated in 3 places with inconsistent approaches. `getRelPath` handles both `/data/assets/` and `data/assets/`; `sources-tab` normalization handles those plus already-canonical; `getSourceLabel` only handles `data/assets/`.
- **Impact**: Maintenance burden; any format change requires updating multiple sites. `getSourceLabel` is broken for `/data/assets/` inputs.
- **Recommended fix**: Extract a single utility function:
  ```ts
  // src/utils/path.ts
  export function toAssetRelPath(path: string): string {
      if (path.startsWith('/data/assets/')) return 'assets/' + path.slice('/data/assets/'.length)
      if (path.startsWith('data/assets/'))  return 'assets/' + path.slice('data/assets/'.length)
      return path  // already canonical
  }
  ```
  Use this in `getRelPath`, `sources-tab` normalization, and `getSourceLabel`.

#### ⚠️ Issue C — `getSourceLabel` checks wrong prefix (dormant bug)

- **Location**: `src/services/sourceManager.ts` lines 125-128
- **What happens**:
  ```ts
  const prefix = 'data/assets/'
  return path.startsWith(prefix) ? path.slice(prefix.length) : path
  ```
  When `scanSource` is called from `sources-tab.svelte` with path `/data/assets/subfolder/`, it does NOT match because the string starts with `/`, not `d`. Returns `/data/assets/subfolder/` as the label instead of `subfolder`.
- **Impact**: **Dormant** — `sourceLabel` on `ImageItem` is never read by any UI component (only `types.ts` declares it, `sourceManager.ts` writes it, but nothing reads it). However, if any future code consumes `sourceLabel`, it would get wrong values.
- **Recommended fix**: Use the shared `toAssetRelPath` utility proposed in Issue B, then strip `assets/` for the label.

---

### Summary

| Aspect | Status |
|--------|--------|
| Config store canonical format | `assets/subfolder` — **correct and consistently used** |
| asset-picker path construction | Internal `/data/assets/...` → canonical `assets/...` on output — **correct** |
| sources-tab normalization | 3-format normalization → canonical — **correct, backward-compatible** |
| `scanAll` in sourceManager | Passes raw `assets/subfolder` to kernel API instead of `/data/assets/subfolder` — **inconsistent but likely works by accident** |
| `getFileUrl` for assets canvas URL | Handles all path formats robustly → `assets/.../img.jpg` — **correct** |
| `openInFileManager` | Correct when `wsDir` has no trailing slash — **works** |
| `getSourceLabel` | Only handles `data/assets/` prefix (no `/data/`) — **dormant bug** |
| Path normalization duplication | Same logic in 3 places — **maintenance risk** |
| `sourceLabel` field | Set but never read in UI — **dead code** |

**Bottom line**: The system works correctly in practice because the stored canonical format (`assets/subfolder`) flows through all the code paths that matter, and `getFileUrl` handles all input variations. The main risks are (A) `scanAll` not normalizing before the kernel API call (fragile, relies on kernel's path resolution behavior), and (B) duplicated normalization logic that could drift. **No critical path is broken.** Nya~♡
</task_result>

Let me present a clean plan.

</details>

## 完整审计结论

存储格式 `assets/title/subfolder2` 已经是统一的规范格式，问题出在 **消耗侧**（`sourceManager.ts scanAll()`）没有把规范格式转换成内核 API 需要的 `/data/assets/...` 路径。

### 识别的 3 个问题

| # | 位置 | 问题 | 严重度 |
|---|------|------|--------|
| A | `sourceManager.ts:22` | 直接传 `assets/subfolder` 给 `readDir` API（缺 `/data/` 前缀） | **Critical** |
| B | 3处重复归一化逻辑 | `asset-picker:115`, `sources-tab:57`, `sourceManager.ts:126` — 各自实现相同逻辑 | **Medium** |
| C | `sourceManager.ts:126` | `getSourceLabel` 只匹配 `data/assets/`，不匹配 `/data/assets/`（但暂时无调用方，dormant） | **Low** |

### 修复计划

**1. 提取 `toAssetRelPath()` 工具函数**

在 `src/utils/` 新建或用现有文件，封装单一职责的归一化：

```ts
// 输入: 任意格式 → 输出: 规范格式 "assets/xxx"
export function toAssetRelPath(path: string): string {
    if (path.startsWith('/data/assets/')) return 'assets/' + path.slice('/data/assets/'.length)
    if (path.startsWith('data/assets/'))  return 'assets/' + path.slice('data/assets/'.length)
    return path
}
```

**2. `sourceManager.ts` 改 2 处**

- `scanAll` 中对 assets 目录补 `/data/` 前缀后传 API（修复 Issue A）
- `getSourceLabel` 改用 `toAssetRelPath`（修复 Issue C）

**3. 现有调用点改用 `toAssetRelPath`**

- `asset-picker.svelte:115` (`getRelPath`)
- `sources-tab.svelte:57-59`（内联归一化）
- `sourceManager.ts:126` (`getSourceLabel`)

### 变更范围

| 文件 | 变更 |
|------|------|
| `src/utils/path.ts` | **新增** `toAssetRelPath()` |
| `src/services/sourceManager.ts` | `scanAll` 补路径前缀 + `getSourceLabel` 改用工具函数 |
| `src/ui/sources/asset-picker.svelte` | `getRelPath` 改用工具函数 |
| `src/ui/settings/sources-tab.svelte` | 内联归一化改用工具函数 |

总计 4 个文件，改动量小，无 API 签名变更。需要我实施吗？ Nya~♡

The user is asking why there are two different path formats: `/data/assets/...` and `data/assets/...` (with and without leading slash). Let me figure out where each comes from.

Let me trace the data flow:

1. **`/data/assets/...`** - This comes from the **asset-picker** component's internal tree node paths. The node paths are constructed as `/data/assets/` + name. This is an "absolute" workspace path format (relative to workspace root).

2. **`data/assets/...`** - This comes from... let me think. Where does `data/assets/` (without leading slash) appear?

Looking at the code in `getFileUrl` (fs.ts:41-42):
```ts
if (rel.startsWith('/data/')) rel = rel.slice(1)  // removes leading /
if (rel.startsWith('data/')) rel = rel.slice(5)     // strips data/ prefix
```

Also in `getSourceLabel` (sourceManager.ts:126):
```ts
const prefix = 'data/assets/'
return path.startsWith(prefix) ? path.slice(prefix.length) : path
```

But wait, `getSourceLabel` only handles `data/assets/` (no leading `/`), not `/data/assets/`. If the path passed to `scanSource` from `sources-tab.svelte` is `/data/assets/subfolder/`, and then `getFileUrl` strips it correctly, but `getSourceLabel` wouldn't match `/data/assets/`. However, `getSourceLabel` is called with the `path` parameter passed to `scanSource`, not with `apiPath`.

Actually, let me re-read. In `scanSource`:

```ts
export async function scanSource(
    type: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets',
    path: string,
): Promise<ImageItem[]> {
    // ...
    for (const name of filenames) {
        const cleanPath = path.endsWith('/') ? path : path + '/'
        const apiPath = `${cleanPath}${name}`
        const url = getFileUrl(apiPath, type)
        items.push({
            sourceLabel: getSourceLabel(type, path),  // path is the original scanSource parameter
        })
    }
}
```

So `getSourceLabel` receives the original `path` parameter:
- From `sources-tab.svelte`: `path = "/data/assets/subfolder/"` → `getSourceLabel('assets', "/data/assets/subfolder/")` → checks `prefix = 'data/assets/'` → `/data/assets/...` does NOT start with `data/assets/` (it starts with `/`) → returns raw path
- From `scanAll`: `path = "assets/subfolder"` → `getSourceLabel('assets', "assets/subfolder")` → checks `prefix = 'data/assets/'` → doesn't match → returns raw path

So `getSourceLabel` is indeed broken for both cases, but since no one reads `sourceLabel`, it's dormant.

Now, why two formats?

Actually the user's question is: why do we have both `/data/assets` and `data/assets`? Let me think about where `data/assets` (without `/`) could come from...

Looking at `getFileUrl`:
```ts
let rel = apiPath
if (rel.startsWith('/data/')) rel = rel.slice(1)    // /data/public/... → data/public/...
if (rel.startsWith('data/')) rel = rel.slice(5)      // data/public/... → public/...
```

So `getFileUrl` handles both formats, but where do these two input formats come from?

- `/data/assets/...` comes from `sources-tab.svelte` which constructs the path as `/data/${normalized}` where `normalized` is `assets/xxx`. Result: `/data/assets/xxx`
- `data/assets/...` could come from... hmm, where?

Actually wait. Looking at the tests:
```
tests/utils/fs.test.ts:94 — getFileUrl('data/assets/wallpaper/img.jpg', 'assets')
```
This tests with `data/assets/...` format. 

But in the actual code, do we ever produce `data/assets/...`? Let me think...

The `pluginAssetsDir` constant might provide a clue. Let me check what value it has.

From `constants.ts` - `pluginAssetsDir` is the upload directory path, something like `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/`. That's a `data/...` format path used for uploads.

For assets, the path construction:
- `asset-picker` uses `/data/assets/...` for internal tree building
- `sources-tab` constructs `/data/assets/...` for `scanSource`
- `scanAll` passes the raw config value `assets/...`

So where does `data/assets/` (no leading `/`) actually appear in production code? 

Looking more carefully... I think `data/assets/` without the leading `/` is just a theoretical variant that is handled defensively in `getFileUrl` and `getSourceLabel`, but might not actually be produced by any current code path. The defensive handling is there "just in case" or is a remnant of older code.

Actually, I should check if there was historical code that used `data/assets/...` format. But for the purpose of answering the user's question:

The two formats come from different "conventions":
- `/data/assets/...` — "absolute" workspace-relative path, used when constructing API paths from knowledge of the workspace structure. The leading `/` means "from workspace root".
- `data/assets/...` — "relative" path format, same as above but without the leading `/`. Sometimes the kernel accepts both (with or without leading `/`).

In practice, the kernel API might accept both `/data/assets/...` and `data/assets/...`. But the safe/conventional format used by the asset-picker and sources-tab is `/data/assets/...`.

The real question from the user is why we need to handle both in the normalization - and I think the answer is simply defensive programming. But for the proposed `toAssetRelPath` utility, handling both makes sense for backward compatibility (in case someone has config values stored in the other format).

Let me give a clear, concise answer.

</details>

两种格式的来源：

- **`/data/assets/...`** — 以 `/` 开头，是「工作空间根目录相对路径」。asset-picker 组件内部构造树节点路径时用这个格式（`"/data/assets/" + name`），sources-tab 在构造 API 路径时也补上 `/` 前缀。这是内核 API 的标准输入格式。

- **`data/assets/...`** — 不以 `/` 开头，但从语义上也是指 `{workspaceDir}/data/assets/...`。`getFileUrl()` 和 `getSourceLabel()` 对它作了防御性处理：

  ```ts
  // getFileUrl 处理两种:
  if (rel.startsWith('/data/')) rel = rel.slice(1)   // /data/... → data/...
  if (rel.startsWith('data/')) rel = rel.slice(5)    // data/...  → ... (strip)
  ```

至于 `data/assets/...` 在 **当前生产代码中是否真的会出现**：我怀疑不会。`asset-picker` 产出的是 `/data/assets/...`，`sources-tab` 也产出 `/data/assets/...`，`assetDirs` 存的是 `assets/...`。`data/assets/` 格式目前没有生产路径产出它，更像是历史遗留的防御性处理。

**结论**：归一化工具函数 `toAssetRelPath()` 保留对 `/data/assets/` 的处理即可。对 `data/assets/` 的处理可以去掉（除非你担心历史配置中有存过这种格式）。

要我去掉 `data/assets/` 那条归一化分支吗？还是保留以防万一？ Nya~♡

### 最终修复计划

**新增 1 个文件：`src/utils/path.ts`**

```ts
/** 将任意 assets 路径归一化为规范存储格式 "assets/xxx" */
export function toAssetRelPath(path: string): string {
    const prefix = '/data/assets/'
    return path.startsWith(prefix) ? 'assets/' + path.slice(prefix.length) : path
}
```

**改 4 处已有代码：**

| 文件 | 原代码 | 改为 |
|------|--------|------|
| `asset-picker.svelte:115-118` | 内联 `getRelPath()` 逻辑 | 调用 `toAssetRelPath()` |
| `sources-tab.svelte:57-59` | 3分支内联归一化 | 调用 `toAssetRelPath()`，只保留 `assets/` → `/data/assets/` 转换 |
| `sourceManager.ts:20-22` | `scanSource('assets', dir)` | 先 `toAssetRelPath(dir)` 再补 `/data/` 前缀传给 API |
| `sourceManager.ts:125-128` | `getSourceLabel` 的 `data/assets/` 匹配 | 用 `toAssetRelPath()` |

<task_result>
Now I have all the data needed. Let me compile the comprehensive audit report.

---

## i18n Audit Report: Complete Findings

### 1. HARDCODED TEXT WITHOUT i18n LOOKUP (5 items — MUST FIX)

These are Chinese text strings rendered directly in the UI with **no** `i18n.xxx ??` fallback pattern at all:

| # | File | Line | Current Hardcoded Text | Suggested i18n Key |
|---|------|------|------------------------|---------------------|
| 1 | `src/ui/settings/theme-tab.svelte` | **63, 102** | `[当前主题]` | `currentThemeLabel` |
| 2 | `src/ui/local-dir-dialog.svelte` | **95** | `发现 {imgCount} 张图片, {vidCount} 个视频 — ✅` | `dirScanResult` |
| 3 | `src/ui/sources/source-list.svelte` | **38** | `(图片: {imageCount} 视频: {videoCount})` | `fileCountSummary` |
| 4 | `src/ui/settings/sources-tab.svelte` | **412** | `( 图片: {imgCount}  视频: {vidCount} )` | `fileCountSummary` (same key, different spacing) |
| 5 | `src/ui/settings/sources-tab.svelte` | **437** | `aria-label="打开文件夹"` | `openFolderLabel` |

**Details:**

* **#1** `[当前主题]` appears twice in `theme-tab.svelte` (lines 63 and 102), once in the light themes card loop and once in the dark themes card loop. It marks the currently active theme. There is no `i18n` lookup at all.

* **#2** In `local-dir-dialog.svelte` line 95, the success message after scanning a directory is completely hardcoded: `发现 {imgCount} 张图片, {vidCount} 个视频 — ✅`. Needs a template-style i18n key similar to `bulkUploadWarning`.

* **#3** `source-list.svelte` line 38: `(图片: {imageCount} 视频: {videoCount})` — inline Chinese text in the source group label.

* **#4** `sources-tab.svelte` line 412: `( 图片: {imgCount}  视频: {vidCount} )` — same pattern but with extra spaces. Items #3 and #4 should share one i18n key (e.g., `fileCountSummary`) with a template like `{img} images, {vid} videos` / `{img} 张图片, {vid} 个视频`.

* **#5** `sources-tab.svelte` line 437: `aria-label="打开文件夹"` — the tooltip text for the "open in file manager" button. This is in the `upload`/`assets`/`local` group rows and has no i18n lookup.

---

### 2. I18N KEY CROSS-REFERENCE BETWEEN zh_CN.json AND en_US.json

**Result: No missing keys.** Both files contain exactly the same 98 keys in the same order.

---

### 3. ALL `i18n.xxx ?? "fallback"` PATTERNS — FALLBACK AUDIT

Below is the complete list of every `i18n.xxx ?? "fallback"` in the codebase. The key exists in **both** zh_CN.json and en_US.json for every entry, meaning the fallback text is only reached when the entire `window.bgCoverPlugin?.i18n` object is unavailable (e.g., plugin not fully loaded).

**None of these fallbacks can be safely removed** — they serve as essential safety nets.

| File | Key Used | Fallback (Chinese) | Key in zh_CN? | Key in en_US? |
|------|----------|-------------------|:---:|:---:|
| **config-tab.svelte** | `currentFile` | "当前背景图片" | ✓ | ✓ |

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

So `window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n = this.i18n`, which is the Plugin's built-in i18n loaded by SiYuan from the `public/i18n/` directory. This is always available when components render because the plugin's `onload()` sets it up before any UI is shown.

Now, the question is: since all keys exist in both zh_CN.json and en_US.json, can we safely remove all the `?? "fallback"` patterns?

The answer is YES — because:
1. `window.bgCoverPlugin.i18n` is set in `onload()` before any UI interaction
2. All keys exist in both language files
3. The `??` fallback patterns are just defensive coding, but the i18n keys should always be available

However, the user said "所有的label也不需要fallback，确保i18n都有的话，是不需要fallback字符串的". So they want me to remove fallbacks and ensure all keys exist.

Let me now present the plan.

</details>

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

Now let me also check the existing fallback `imageCount` and `videoCount` keys. In `zh_CN.json`, `"imageCount": "图片"` and `"videoCount": "视频"`, but in `en_US.json`, `"imageCount": "Images"` and `"videoCount": "Videos"`. These are used in several places with template-like formatting.

Wait, let me think about `fileCountSummary`. The template needs to support parameter substitution (like `${var}` style or positional). Looking at how the i18n system works in SiYuan, looking at the comment in AGENTS.md: "运行时: 思源自动读 i18n/ 目录注入 this.i18n" and "代码中使用: this.i18n.keyName 直接访问，支持 ${var} 模板插值"

But in the code, they access i18n via `(window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.i18n ?? {}`. This is `this.i18n` from the Plugin class, which should support template interpolation.

However, looking at the existing `bulkUploadWarning`: `"此次将上传 {count} 张图片/视频，确定全部上传吗？"` — it uses `{count}` syntax, not `${count}`.

Let me check how `bulkUploadWarning` is used in the code:
```typescript
i18n.bulkUploadWarning.replace("{count}", `${files.length}`)
```

So they use manual `.replace()` for parameter substitution. Good.

Now for `fileCountSummary`, I need to account for the fact that both `source-list.svelte` and `sources-tab.svelte` use it with slightly different spacing. Let me look at the exact patterns:

source-list.svelte: `(图片: {imageCount} 视频: {videoCount})`
sources-tab.svelte: `( 图片: {imgCount}  视频: {vidCount} )`

The template can be something like `(图片: {img}  视频: {vid})` — the padding spaces can be in the template. But source-list uses tighter spacing.

Let me use a clean template without extra spaces and let the component decide:
zh_CN: `"fileCountSummary": "图片: {img} 视频: {vid}"`
en_US: `"fileCountSummary": "Images: {img} Videos: {vid}"`

Then in the UI code:
```typescript
// source-list.svelte
({i18n.fileCountSummary.replace('{img}', `${imageCount}`).replace('{vid}', `${videoCount}`)})

// sources-tab.svelte  
( {i18n.fileCountSummary.replace('{img}', `${imgCount}`).replace('{vid}', `${vidCount}`)} )
```

Wait, but the user said "所有的label也不需要fallback". So I also need to remove fallsbacks. Let me look at how i18n is accessed in the Svelte files — it's `const i18n = (window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.i18n ?? {}` at the top of every component.

If I remove the `?? {}`, and the plugin hasn't loaded yet, the component will crash with `Cannot read property ... of undefined`. However, since `bgCoverPlugin.i18n` is set in `onload()` before any UI interaction, this should be safe.

But wait, the user wants all fallbacks removed. Let me follow the user's instruction.

Actually, I need to be more careful. Some files use `i18n` as a local const with `?? {}` default, and some use it inline. Let me consolidate the approach. I'll keep `const i18n = (window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.i18n ?? {}` (the `?? {}` is on the outer `bgCoverPlugin`, not on individual keys) so the `.replace()` calls don't crash. This is the structural safety net. Then remove the `?? "fallback"` on individual key access.

For example:
```typescript
// Keep this safety net
const i18n = (window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.i18n ?? {}
// But change this - remove fallback
<span>{i18n.currentFile ?? "当前背景图片"}</span>  →  <span>{i18n.currentFile}</span>
```

Wait, but what happens when `i18n = {}` (the outer safety net triggers)? Then `i18n.currentFile` is `undefined`, and the Svelte template will render `undefined` as text. That's not ideal but acceptable because it only happens in extreme crash scenarios.

Actually, let me re-read the user's instruction: "另外，所有的label也不需要fallback，确保i18n都有的话，是不需要fallback字符串的"

They specifically say labels don't need fallbacks if all i18n keys exist. This means removing `?? "some fallback text"` after each `i18n.xxx` access. Not removing the outer `?? {}` safety net.

OK, let me plan the implementation:

1. Update both i18n JSON files:
   - Add: `currentThemeLabel`, `dirScanResult`, `fileCountSummary`, `openFolderLabel`
   - Remove: `switchInterval`, `disabledThemesTitle`, `confirmUpload`

2. Fix hardcoded strings (5 places)

3. Remove `?? "fallback"` from all i18n accesses

Let me now do the glob search to find ALL i18n uses with fallbacks first, so I know exactly what to change.

Actually, let me use the task approach to find and replace all at once. But since each file is independent, let me do it file by file.

Let me start with the JSON files and the hardcoded string fixes first, then tackle the fallback removal across all files.

Let me create a comprehensive approach:

Step 1: Update i18n JSONs (add 4 keys, remove 3)
Step 2: Fix theme-tab.svelte hardcoded strings
Step 3: Fix local-dir-dialog.svelte hardcoded string
Step 4: Fix source-list.svelte hardcoded string
Step 5: Fix sources-tab.svelte hardcoded strings
Step 6: Remove all `?? "fallback"` from all .svelte and .ts files

For step 6, I'll need to search all files systematically. Let me use a subagent for that.

Actually, let me just do it file by file. I'll read each file, find patterns, and edit. Let me start with the JSON files first since they're simplest.

<content>
1: <script lang="ts">
2:     import { onMount } from "svelte"
3:     import { configStore } from "../../stores/config"
4:     import { getInstalledThemes, getCurrentThemeInfo } from "../../utils/theme"
5:     import type { ThemeInfo } from "../../utils/theme"
6: 
7:     const i18n = (window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.i18n ?? {}
8: 
9:     let disabledThemes = $state(configStore.get("disabledThemes"))
10:     let lightItems = $state<ThemeInfo[]>([])
11:     let darkItems = $state<ThemeInfo[]>([])
12:     let currentMode = $state(0)
13:     let currentThemeName = $state('')
14: 
15:     onMount(() => {
16:         const [light, dark] = getInstalledThemes()
17:         lightItems = light
18:         darkItems = dark
19:         const [mode, name] = getCurrentThemeInfo()
20:         currentMode = mode
21:         currentThemeName = name
22:     })
23: 
24:     $effect(() => {
25:         disabledThemes = configStore.get("disabledThemes")
26:     })
27: 
28:     function toggleTheme(mode: 'light' | 'dark', name: string) {
29:         const dt = configStore.get("disabledThemes")
30:         const key = mode === 'light' ? 'light' : 'dark'
31:         const list = [...dt[key]]
32:         const idx = list.indexOf(name)
33:         if (idx >= 0) list.splice(idx, 1)
34:         else list.push(name)
35:         configStore.setAndSave("disabledThemes", { ...dt, [key]: list })
36:         ;(window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.plugin?.applyThemeShield?.()
37:     }
38: </script>
39: 
40: <div class="config__tab-container" data-name="theme">
41:     <div class="config-bazaar__panel">
42: 
43:         <div class="fn__flex config-bazaar__title">
44:             <div>{i18n.lightThemes ?? "浅色主题"}</div>
45:         </div>
46:         <div class="config-bazaar__content">
47:             {#if lightItems.length === 0}
48:                 <div style="color: var(--b3-theme-on-surface); padding: 8px;">
49:                     {i18n.noLightThemes ?? "暂无已安装的浅色主题"}
50:                 </div>
51:             {:else}
52:                 <div class="b3-cards">
53:                     {#each lightItems as theme (theme.name)}
54:                         <div class="b3-card b3-card--wrap">
55:                             <div class="fn__flex-1 fn__flex-column">
56:                                 <div class="b3-card__info b3-card__info--left fn__flex-1">
57:                                     <span
58:                                         style:color={currentMode === 0 && currentThemeName === theme.name
59:                                             ? 'var(--b3-theme-primary)' : ''}
60:                                     >
61:                                         {theme.name}
62:                                         {#if currentMode === 0 && currentThemeName === theme.name}
63:                                             [当前主题]
64:                                         {/if}
65:                                     </span>
66:                                     <div class="b3-card__desc">{theme.label}</div>
67:                                 </div>
68:                             </div>
69:                             <div class="b3-card__actions b3-card__actions--right">
70:                                 <span class="fn__space"></span>
71:                                 <input class="b3-switch fn__flex-center" type="checkbox"
72:                                     checked={disabledThemes.light.includes(theme.name)}
73:                                     onchange={() => toggleTheme('light', theme.name)}
74:                                 />
75:                             </div>
76:                         </div>
77:                     {/each}
78:                 </div>
79:             {/if}
80:         </div>

16:     let vidCount = $state(0)
17:     let errorMsg = $state("")
18:     let debounceTimer: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null = null
19: 
20:     async function doCheck(p: string) {
21:         if (!p) {
22:             validDir = false
23:             errorMsg = ""
24:             imgCount = 0
25:             vidCount = 0
26:             return
27:         }
28:         checking = true
29:         errorMsg = ""
30:         validDir = false
31:         imgCount = 0
32:         vidCount = 0
33: 
34:         const fsp = (window as any).require?.('fs/promises')
35:         if (!fsp) {
36:             errorMsg = i18n.notDesktop ?? "当前非桌面端，不支持本地目录"
37:             checking = false
38:             return
39:         }
40: 
41:         try {
42:             await fsp.access(p)
43:         } catch {
44:             errorMsg = i18n.pathNotExist ?? "路径不存在或无法访问"
45:             checking = false
46:             return
47:         }
48: 
49:         try {
50:             const entries = await fsp.readdir(p, { withFileTypes: true })
51:             for (const e of entries) {
52:                 if (!e.isFile()) continue
53:                 const t = classifyFileType(e.name)
54:                 if (t === 'image') imgCount++
55:                 else if (t === 'video') vidCount++
56:             }
57:             if (imgCount + vidCount === 0) {
58:                 errorMsg = i18n.noValidFiles ?? "该目录下未发现支持的图片/视频文件"
59:             } else {
60:                 validDir = true
61:             }
62:         } catch (e: any) {
63:             errorMsg = `${i18n.readDirFailed ?? "读取目录失败"}: ${e.message}`
64:         }
65:         checking = false
66:     }
67: 
68:     function handleInput() {
69:         if (debounceTimer) clearTimeout(debounceTimer)
70:         debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => doCheck(pathInput.trim()), 500)
71:     }
72: 
73:     function confirm() {
74:         onConfirm?.(pathInput.trim())
75:     }

15: 
16:     const uploadItems = await scanSource('upload', pluginAssetsDir)

18:     debug(`${ENGINE} scanAll upload: ${uploadItems.length} 个文件`)

31:             if (!ok) {

44:     return results

47: export async function scanSource(
48:     type: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets',
49:     path: string,
50: ): Promise<ImageItem[]> {
51:     const filenames = type === 'local'
52:         ? await readLocalDir(path)
53:         : await readDirKernel(path)
54: 
55:     const items: ImageItem[] = []
56:     const skipped: string[] = []
57: 
58:     for (const name of filenames) {
59:         const fileType = classifyFileType(name)
60: 
61:         if (fileType === null) {
62:             skipped.push(name)
63:             continue
64:         }
65: 
66:         const cleanPath = path.endsWith('/') ? path : path + '/'

72:             url,

75:             sourceType: type,

77:         })
78:     }
79: 
80:     if (skipped.length > 0) {
81:         debug(`${ENGINE} scanSource[${type}] 跳过不可识别的文件: [${skipped.join(', ')}]`)
82:     }
83: 
84:     return items
85: }

87: export function pickRandom(items: ImageItem[], excludeUrl?: string | null): ImageItem | null {
88:     if (items.length === 0) return null
89: 
90:     if (excludeUrl) {
91:         const filtered = items.filter(item => item.url !== excludeUrl)
92:         if (filtered.length === 0) return null
93:         const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * filtered.length)
94:         return filtered[idx]
95:     }
96: 
97:     const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * items.length)
98:     return items[idx]
99: }
100: 
101: export async function validatePath(path: string): Promise<boolean> {
102:     if (path.length === 0) return false
103: 
104:     if (isDesktop()) {
105:         try {
106:             await (window as any).require('fs/promises').access(path)
107:             return true
108:         } catch {
109:             return false
110:         }
111:     }
112: 
113:     try {
114:         await readDirKernel(path)
115:         return true
116:     } catch {
117:         return false
118:     }
119: }
120: 
121: function getSourceLabel(type: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets', path: string): string {
122:     switch (type) {
123:         case 'upload':
124:             return 'upload'
125:         case 'assets': {
126:             const prefix = 'data/assets/'
127:             return path.startsWith(prefix) ? path.slice(prefix.length) : path
128:         }
129:         case 'local':
130:             return path
131:     }
132: }

1: import { fetchSyncPost } from "siyuan"

4: interface IResponse {
5:     code: number
6:     msg: string
7:     data: any
8: }

11:     isDir: boolean
12:     name: string
13: }
14: 
15: async function request(url: string, data: any): Promise<any> {
16:     const res: IResponse = await fetchSyncPost(url, data)
17:     return res.code === 0 ? res.data : null
18: }
19: 
20: export async function readDir(path: string): Promise<string[]> {
21:     const data = await request("/api/file/readDir", { path })
22:     if (!Array.isArray(data)) return []
23:     return (data as IDirItem[])
24:         .filter(item => !item.isDir)
25:         .map(item => item.name)
26: }
27: 
28: export async function fileExistsRemote(path: string): Promise<boolean> {
29:     if (!path) return false
30:     const parentPath = path.substring(0, path.lastIndexOf('/'))
31:     const targetName = path.substring(path.lastIndexOf('/') + 1)
32:     const files = await readDir(parentPath)
33:     return files.includes(targetName)
34: }
35: 
36: export async function readDirItems(path: string): Promise<IDirItem[]> {
37:     const data = await request("/api/file/readDir", { path })
38:     if (!Array.isArray(data)) return []
39:     return data as IDirItem[]
40: }
41: 
42: export async function putFile(path: string, file: File | Blob): Promise<boolean> {
43:     const formData = new FormData()
44:     formData.append("path", path)
45:     formData.append("isDir", "false")
46:     formData.append("modTime", Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000).toString())
47:     formData.append("file", file)
48: 
49:     const res: IResponse = await fetchSyncPost("/api/file/putFile", formData)
50:     return res.code === 0
51: }
52: 
53: export async function removeFile(path: string): Promise<boolean> {
54:     const res: IResponse = await fetchSyncPost("/api/file/removeFile", { path })
55:     return res.code === 0
56: }
57: 
58: export async function downloadUrl(url: string, destPath: string): Promise<boolean> {
59:     try {
60:         const response = await fetch(url)
61:         if (!response.ok) return false
62:         const blob = await response.blob()
63:         return await putFile(destPath, blob)
64:     } catch (err: any) {
65:         debug('[bgCover] api.ts downloadUrl 失败:', url, err.message)
66:         return false
67:     }
68: }

126:         const active = !configStore.get("activate")
127:         log("[bgCover] toggleBackground:", active ? "activated" : "deactivated")
128:         configStore.setAndSave("activate", active)
129:         if (active) {
130:             createBgLayer()
131:             this.applyBackground()
132:         } else {

138:         const assetDirs = configStore.get("assetDirs")
139:         const localFolders = configStore.get("localFolders")
140:         const pool = await scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders)
141:         if (pool.length === 0) {
142:             log("[bgCover] randomSelect: pool is empty, nothing to pick")
143:             return
144:         }
145:         const exclude = pool.length > 1 ? configStore.get("currentFile") : null
146:         const item = pickRandom(pool, exclude)
147:         if (!item) return
148:         log("[bgCover] randomSelect: picked", item.name, "from", pool.length, "items")
149:         configStore.set("currentFile", item.url)
150:         configStore.save()

152:             renderImage(item.url)
153:         } else {
154:             renderVideo(item.url)
155:         }
156:         changeOpacity(configStore.get("opacity"))
157:         changeBlur(configStore.get("blur"))

166:             if (!currentFile) {
167:                 debug("[bgCover] applyBackground: currentFile is null, skip render")
168:                 return
169:             }
170: 
171:             const ext = '.' + (currentFile.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
172:             debug("[bgCover] applyBackground: ext =", ext)
173:             if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) {
174:                 debug("[bgCover] applyBackground: -> renderVideo")
175:                 renderVideo(currentFile)
176:             } else if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext)) {
177:                 debug("[bgCover] applyBackground: -> renderImage")
178:                 renderImage(currentFile)
179:             } else {
180:                 console.warn(`[bgCover] applyBackground: unknown extension "${ext}" for ${currentFile}`)
181:                 return
182:             }
183:         } finally {
184:             const opacity = configStore.get("opacity")
185:             const blur = configStore.get("blur")
186:             const px = configStore.get("positionX")
187:             const py = configStore.get("positionY")
188:             debug("[bgCover] applyBackground: changeOpacity =", opacity, "blur =", blur, "pos =", px, py)
189:             changeOpacity(opacity)
190:             changeBlur(blur)
191:             changePosition(px, py)
192:         }
193: 
194:         const interval = configStore.get("autoRefreshTime")
195:         stopAutoRefresh()
196:         if (interval > 0) {
197:             startAutoRefresh(() => this.randomSelect(), interval * 60000)
198:         }
199:     }
200: 
201:     applyThemeShield() {
202:         if (!configStore.get("activate")) return
203:         if (isCurrentThemeDisabled(configStore.get("disabledThemes"))) {
204:             log("[bgCover] applyThemeShield: theme disabled, hiding")
205:             setVisible(false)
206:         } else {
207:             log("[bgCover] applyThemeShield: theme enabled, showing")
208:             createBgLayer()
209:             this.applyBackground()
210:         }
211:     }
212: }

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

Now I have all the key pieces. Let me analyze the flow carefully.

**The user's question**: Why does `scanAll` report 0 files for an assets directory but the source-list UI can see files in the same directory?

Let me trace through the code:

### `scanAll` flow:

1. `scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders)` is called from `index.ts` (lines 77, 140)
2. For each `dir` in `assetDirs`, it calls `scanSource('assets', dir)` (line 22)
3. `scanSource` calls `readDirKernel(path)` for non-local types (line 53)
4. `readDirKernel` = `readDir` from `api.ts`
5. In `api.ts`, `readDir` calls `request("/api/file/readDir", { path })` which calls `fetchSyncPost`
6. It filters `!item.isDir` and maps to `item.name`

### Key question: What path is passed in `assetDirs`?

The `assetDirs` config value comes from the configuration store. When a user links an assets directory, the path stored in the config is whatever path the user selected.

Looking at the `constants.ts`: `pluginAssetsDir = '/data/public/${packageName}/'`

For assets type, the path should be something like `data/assets/...` (relative to the workspace).

Now, the possible issue: When `readDir` is called via `fetchSyncPost("/api/file/readDir", { path })`, the path must be a valid kernel path. The `/api/file/readDir` API expects paths relative to the workspace root (like `data/assets/myfolder` or `/data/assets/myfolder`).

### Looking at `source-list.svelte`:

It receives `files: ImageItem[]` as a prop. The `files` array is populated elsewhere (not shown in source-list.svelte itself - it's a purely presentational component).

To understand how source-list gets its data, I need to find where `source-list.svelte` is used and how `files` are populated.

Let me search for where source-list is imported/used.

</details>

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

Now I have the complete picture. Let me trace through both code paths for an assets directory and identify the discrepancy.

### Path 1: `scanAll` (in index.ts / sourceManager.ts)

In `index.ts` line 77:
```typescript
const assetDirs = configStore.get("assetDirs")
const localFolders = configStore.get("localFolders")
const pool = await scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders)
```

In `sourceManager.ts` lines 20-25:
```typescript
for (const dir of assetDirs) {
    if (dir.length === 0) continue
    const items = await scanSource('assets', dir)
    results.push(...items)
}
```

So `scanSource('assets', dir)` is called with `dir` directly from the config store. The `dir` value is the raw value stored in the config's `assetDirs` array.

Now, what value is stored in `assetDirs`? Let's look at how it's set.

### How assetDirs are stored

In `AssetPicker` (asset-picker.svelte), when a user picks an assets directory, and then `addAssetFolder(dir)` is called in `sources-tab.svelte` line 131-138:

```typescript
function addAssetFolder(dir: string) {
    if (!dir) return
    const dirs = [...configStore.get("assetDirs"), dir]
    configStore.set("assetDirs", dirs)
    configStore.save()
    refreshAll()
}
```

The `dir` comes from the AssetPicker's `onConfirm(paths: string[])`. Let me check asset-picker.svelte.

### Path in sources-tab's refreshAll (the UI-side `scanSource` call for assets):

```typescript
// sources-tab.svelte lines 54-73
const assetDirs = configStore.get("assetDirs")
for (const dir of assetDirs) {
    if (!dir) continue
    const normalized = dir.startsWith('/data/assets/') ? `assets/${dir.slice('/data/assets/'.length)}`
        : dir.startsWith('data/assets/') ? `assets/${dir.slice('data/assets/'.length)}`
        : dir
    const path = `/data/${normalized}`
    const label = normalized.startsWith('assets/') ? normalized.slice('assets/'.length) : normalized
    const files = await scanSource('assets', path + '/')
    newGroups.push({...})
}
```

Here, the path constructed for `scanSource('assets', ...)` is: **`/data/assets/<folder_name>/`**

But in `sourceManager.ts` `scanAll`, the path passed to `scanSource` is the raw `dir` from config, which might be something like:
- `assets/<folder_name>` (relative path without `/data/` prefix)
- or perhaps just `<folder_name>`

### The critical difference:

- **`sources-tab.svelte` `refreshAll`**: Always constructs the path as `/data/assets/<folder_name>/` (with `/data/` prefix and trailing `/`)
- **`sourceManager.ts` `scanAll`**: Uses the raw `dir` value from config directly, which might or might not have the `/data/` prefix

The `/api/file/readDir` API needs a path relative to the workspace root. If the stored config value is something like `assets/myfolder`, the API call with `path: "assets/myfolder"` might fail because the API expects paths like `data/assets/myfolder`.

Wait, let me re-examine. The `readDir` in `api.ts`:
```typescript
export async function readDir(path: string): Promise<string[]> {
    const data = await request("/api/file/readDir", { path })
    ...
}
```

This sends `{ path: dir }` to `/api/file/readDir`. The SiYuan kernel API expects the path relative to the data directory. According to the siyuan API reference, the path format for assets would be like `data/assets/myfolder`.

But the stored config value might be just `assets/myfolder` (without `data/` prefix). This would cause the API to look in the wrong place.

Let me verify by checking asset-picker.svelte to see what path format it returns.

</details>

Now I have the complete picture. Let me trace through the exact flow.

### The Bug: Path mismatch between `scanAll` and `sources-tab.refreshAll`

**Asset picker returns path format:** `assets/<folder_name>` (relative, no `/data/` prefix)

This is from `getRelPath()` in `asset-picker.svelte` (lines 115-119):
```typescript
function getRelPath(fullPath: string): string {
    if (fullPath.startsWith('/data/assets/')) return `assets/${fullPath.slice('/data/assets/'.length)}`
    if (fullPath.startsWith('data/assets/')) return `assets/${fullPath.slice('data/assets/'.length)}`
    return fullPath
}
```

So when user picks e.g. `/data/assets/bg/`, `getRelPath` returns `assets/bg/`.

This value is then passed to `onConfirm([rel])`, and then to `addAssetFolder(dir)` in `sources-tab.svelte` line 131, which stores `assets/bg/` in the config's `assetDirs` array.

**Now in `sourceManager.ts` `scanAll` (line 22):**
```typescript
for (const dir of assetDirs) {
    if (dir.length === 0) continue
    const items = await scanSource('assets', dir)  // dir = "assets/bg/"
    ...
}
```

`scanSource('assets', "assets/bg/")` calls `readDirKernel("assets/bg/")` which calls `request("/api/file/readDir", { path: "assets/bg/" })`.

**The SiYuan kernel `/api/file/readDir` API** expects paths relative to the workspace data directory. The actual physical structure in the workspace is `data/assets/bg/`. So the API would need `data/assets/bg/` as the path, not `assets/bg/`.

**But in `sources-tab.svelte` `refreshAll` (lines 54-73):**
```typescript
const assetDirs = configStore.get("assetDirs")
for (const dir of assetDirs) {
    if (!dir) continue
    const normalized = dir.startsWith('/data/assets/') ? `assets/${dir.slice('/data/assets/'.length)}`
        : dir.startsWith('data/assets/') ? `assets/${dir.slice('data/assets/'.length)}`
        : dir
    const path = `/data/${normalized}`  // path = "/data/assets/bg/"
    ...
    const files = await scanSource('assets', path + '/')  // scanSource('assets', "/data/assets/bg/")
}
```

So in `refreshAll`, the path is normalized to `/data/assets/bg/`, which correctly resolves in the kernel API.

**In `scanAll`, however**, the raw config value `assets/bg/` is passed directly without any normalization/prefixing. This means the kernel API is looking for `assets/bg/` relative to the workspace root, which doesn't exist - it should be `data/assets/bg/`.

Wait, but looking at the `readDir` API definition in `api.ts`:
```typescript
export async function readDir(path: string): Promise<string[]> {
    const data = await request("/api/file/readDir", { path })
    ...
}
```

And in the siyuan API docs/source, the `path` parameter for `/api/file/readDir` appears to accept paths like `data/assets/...`. Let me check if maybe the API silently prepends `data/`...

Actually, I need to think about this more carefully. The `request` function calls `fetchSyncPost(url, data)` which does an HTTP POST. The siyuan kernel path handling...

Let me think about how the `readDir` works for the `upload` source type: `pluginAssetsDir = '/data/public/${packageName}/'`. That's passed as `scanSource('upload', '/data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/')`, which calls `readDir('/data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/')`. This works because the actual files are stored at `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/` in the workspace.

Now for assets, the actual files are stored at `data/assets/<folder>/` in the workspace. If the API needs paths relative to workspace root, then `data/assets/bg/` would work but `assets/bg` wouldn't.

Let me check what the actual siyuan kernel API expects... Actually, looking at the code for `asset-picker.svelte` line 51:
```typescript
const items = await readDirItems("/data/assets/")
```

It works with `/data/assets/` prefix. But in `sourceManager.scanAll`, the stored config value is `assets/bg/` (without `/data/` prefix).

The core of the bug is:

1. `asset-picker` returns `assets/<folder>` (via `getRelPath`)
2. Config stores `assets/<folder>`
3. `sources-tab.refreshAll` normalizes it to `/data/assets/<folder>/` before calling `scanSource`
4. `sourceManager.scanAll` passes the raw config value `assets/<folder>` directly to `scanSource`
5. `scanSource` calls `readDir("assets/<folder>")` which fails because the kernel expects `data/assets/<folder>` or `/data/assets/<folder>`

So `scanAll` gets 0 files because the API call fails (returns empty `[]` on error).

The fix would be to normalize the path in `scanAll` (or in `scanSource`) the same way `sources-tab.svelte` does in `refreshAll`.

Actually wait, let me look more carefully at `scanAll` again:

```typescript
export async function scanAll(
    assetDirs: string[] = [],
    localFolders: string[] = [],
): Promise<ImageItem[]> {
    const results: ImageItem[] = []

    const uploadItems = await scanSource('upload', pluginAssetsDir)
    results.push(...uploadItems)

    for (const dir of assetDirs) {
        if (dir.length === 0) continue
        const items = await scanSource('assets', dir)
        results.push(...items)
    }
    ...
}
```

Yes, `dir` is the raw config value. The paths stored in config might be:
- New format (from asset-picker): `assets/bg/` or `assets/bg`
- Potentially old format (migrated from earlier config): could be `/data/assets/bg/` or `data/assets/bg/`

The `sources-tab.refreshAll` handles all these formats with its normalization logic. But `scanAll` does not.

Now wait, let me also see if there's an `addAssetFolder` flow that might store a different format. Looking at `sources-tab.svelte` line 131:
```typescript
function addAssetFolder(dir: string) {
    ...
    const dirs = [...configStore.get("assetDirs"), dir]
    configStore.set("assetDirs", dirs)
    ...
}
```

And `dir` comes from the asset-picker's `onConfirm` callback, which calls `getRelPath` to convert to `assets/<folder>` format.

So the stored format is consistently `assets/<folder>`. And the problem is that `scanAll` doesn't normalize this before calling `scanSource`.

Let me also verify: in `scanSource` line 53:
```typescript
const filenames = type === 'local'
    ? await readLocalDir(path)
    : await readDirKernel(path)
```

And `readDir` in `api.ts` line 20-26:
```typescript
export async function readDir(path: string): Promise<string[]> {
    const data = await request("/api/file/readDir", { path })
    if (!Array.isArray(data)) return []
    return (data as IDirItem[])
        .filter(item => !item.isDir)
        .map(item => item.name)
}
```

If the API fails, it returns `null` from `request`, then the `!Array.isArray(data)` check makes it return `[]`. No error is thrown to the caller - it silently returns an empty array.

So the chain of events is:
1. `scanAll` is called with `assetDirs = ["assets/bg"]`
2. `scanSource('assets', "assets/bg")` is called
3. `readDirKernel("assets/bg")` calls `request("/api/file/readDir", { path: "assets/bg" })`
4. The kernel either returns an error (code != 0) or data = null/not an array
5. `readDir` returns `[]`
6. `scanSource` returns `[]`
7. `scanAll` reports 0 files

Meanwhile, `sources-tab.refreshAll` does the normalization and succeeds.

The fix: Either normalize the path in `scanAll` (matching the logic in `sources-tab.refreshAll`) or normalize in `scanSource` for 'assets' type. The cleaner approach would be to have a single source of truth for path normalization.

Now let me also consider: there's a `getFileUrl` function that constructs the canvas url. For assets type:
```typescript
export function getFileUrl(apiPath: string, sourceType: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets'): string {
    ...
    let rel = apiPath
    if (rel.startsWith('/data/')) rel = rel.slice(1)
    if (rel.startsWith('data/')) rel = rel.slice(5)
    else if (rel.startsWith('/')) rel = rel.slice(1)
    return rel
}
```

For an assets file at path `assets/bg/img.jpg`, `getFileUrl` returns `assets/bg/img.jpg`. This is correct for canvas rendering because the SiYuan webview serves `assets/` paths directly.

But wait, if the `readDir` call had succeeded with a normalized path like `/data/assets/bg/`, then `apiPath` would be `/data/assets/bg/img.jpg`, and `getFileUrl` would strip the `/data/` prefix (first condition matches: `startsWith('/data/')`, then `rel = rel.slice(1)` → `data/assets/bg/img.jpg`, then second condition: `startsWith('data/')`, `rel = rel.slice(5)` → `assets/bg/img.jpg`). So the URL would still be correct.

This confirms the bug: the path normalization only needs to happen before the `readDir` API call, not for URL construction. The best fix location is in `scanSource` or `scanAll` before calling `readDirKernel`.

**Summary of findings:**

The root cause is in `src/services/sourceManager.ts`, function `scanAll` (line 22): it passes raw config values (`assets/<folder>`) directly to `scanSource` → `readDir`, while the SiYuan kernel `/api/file/readDir` API requires paths with the `data/` (or `/data/`) prefix (e.g., `data/assets/<folder>/`).

The UI (`sources-tab.svelte` `refreshAll`) avoids this bug because it normalizes the path:
```typescript
const normalized = dir.startsWith('/data/assets/') ? ...
const path = `/data/${normalized}`
const files = await scanSource('assets', path + '/')
```

But `scanAll` in `sourceManager.ts` skips this normalization entirely and uses the raw config value.

This means:
- **`randomSelect()` in `index.ts`** (called on startup and via hotkey) uses `scanAll` → gets 0 files for assets sources
- **`openSetting("sources")` UI** uses `refreshAll` → correctly sees files

The fix should be to add the same normalization logic in `scanAll` (or in `scanSource` before the `readDirKernel` call).

</details>

Now I have the complete picture. Here is my analysis:

---

## Root Cause Analysis: `scanAll` reports 0 files for assets directories

### The Bug: Path format mismatch

The stored config value for an asset directory (as returned by `asset-picker.svelte`'s `getRelPath()`) is `assets/<folder_name>` — note: **no `/data/` prefix**.

| Code path | Path passed to `readDir` API | Result |
|-----------|------------------------------|--------|
| **`sources-tab.svelte` `refreshAll()`** (lines 57-61) | `/data/assets/<folder>/` | ✅ Works |
| **`sourceManager.ts` `scanAll()`** (line 22) | `assets/<folder>` (raw config value) | ❌ Fails |

### Why it fails

`scanAll` passes the raw config value directly to `scanSource`:

```typescript
// sourceManager.ts:22 — NO normalization
const items = await scanSource('assets', dir)  // dir = "assets/bg"
```

This flows into `readDir()` in `api.ts`, which calls:
```
POST /api/file/readDir { path: "assets/bg" }
```

The SiYuan kernel's `/api/file/readDir` API requires paths relative to the workspace root. An assets folder physically lives at `data/assets/bg/` in the workspace. The API does **not** find `assets/bg` as a valid path, so it returns an error (`code != 0`). In `readDir()` (line 22), the `!Array.isArray(data)` guard catches the error and silently returns `[]`. No exception is thrown.

Meanwhile, `sources-tab.svelte` `refreshAll()` (lines 57-61) normalizes the same config value **before** the API call:

```typescript
// sources-tab.svelte:57-61 — NORMALIZES the path
const normalized = dir.startsWith('/data/assets/') ? `assets/${dir.slice('/data/assets/'.length)}`
    : dir.startsWith('data/assets/') ? `assets/${dir.slice('data/assets/'.length)}`
    : dir
const path = `/data/${normalized}`            // → "/data/assets/bg"
const files = await scanSource('assets', path + '/')  // → "/data/assets/bg/"
```

This produces `/data/assets/bg/`, which the kernel API correctly resolves.

### Impact

All callers of `scanAll` are affected:

| Caller (in `index.ts`) | Trigger | Consequence |
|------------------------|---------|-------------|
| `onload()` line 77 | Plugin startup, when `currentFile` is null | Pool is empty → falls back to default background |
| `randomSelect()` line 140 | `⇧⌘F7` hotkey / topbar "随机抽一张" | Pool is empty → "pool is empty, nothing to pick" |

But opening the Settings UI → Sources tab works fine because it calls `refreshAll()`, which does normalize.

### Where the fix belongs

The normalization should be added in **`scanAll` (or `scanSource`)** — either way makes it consistent. The ideal fix matches the normalization logic that already exists in `sources-tab.svelte:57-61`:

```typescript
// In sourceManager.ts, before calling scanSource for asset type dirs:
for (const dir of assetDirs) {
    if (dir.length === 0) continue
    const normalized = dir.startsWith('/data/assets/') ? `assets/${dir.slice('/data/assets/'.length)}`
        : dir.startsWith('data/assets/') ? `assets/${dir.slice('data/assets/'.length)}`
        : dir
    const path = `/data/${normalized}`
    const items = await scanSource('assets', path + '/')
    ...
}
```

> **Note:** The `getFileUrl()` in `fs.ts` handles both `/data/`-prefixed and unprefixed paths correctly (strips the prefix for canvas CSS), so normalizing the path for the `readDir` API call won't break URL construction.

Nya~♡

65:             })
66:         }
67:         roots.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name))
68:         loading = false
69:     })
70: 
71:     async function expandChild(node: DirNode) {
72:         if (node.open) {
73:             node.open = false
74:             return
75:         }
76: 
77:         if (!node.loaded) {
78:             log("[bgCover] assetPicker expand:", node.name)
79:             node.imageCount = 0
80:             node.videoCount = 0
81:             node.children = []
82: 
83:             const items = await readDirItems(node.path + '/')
84:             for (const child of items) {
85:                 if (child.isDir) {
86:                     const childPath = node.path + '/' + child.name
87:                     const { imageCount, videoCount, hasSubdirs } = await scanDir(childPath)
88:                     node.children.push({
89:                         name: child.name,
90:                         path: childPath,
91:                         imageCount,
92:                         videoCount,
93:                         children: [],
94:                         open: false,
95:                         loaded: false,
96:                         hasSubdirs,
97:                     })
98:                 } else {
99:                     const type = classifyFileType(child.name)
100:                     if (type === 'image') node.imageCount++
101:                     else if (type === 'video') node.videoCount++
102:                 }
103:             }
104:             node.children.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name))
105:             node.loaded = true
106:         }
107: 
108:         node.open = true
109:     }
110: 
111:     function selectDir(path: string, total: number) {
112:         if (total > 0) selectedDir = path
113:     }
114: 
115:     function getRelPath(fullPath: string): string {
116:         if (fullPath.startsWith('/data/assets/')) return `assets/${fullPath.slice('/data/assets/'.length)}`
117:         if (fullPath.startsWith('data/assets/')) return `assets/${fullPath.slice('data/assets/'.length)}`
118:         return fullPath
119:     }
120: 
121:     function confirm() {
122:         if (!selectedDir) return
123:         const rel = getRelPath(selectedDir)
124:         log("[bgCover] assetPicker confirm:", rel)
125:         onConfirm?.([rel])
126:     }
127: 
128:     function isAlreadyAdded(nodePath: string): boolean {
129:         return configStore.get("assetDirs").includes(getRelPath(nodePath))
130:     }
131: </script>
132: 
133: <div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 8px; padding: 8px; width: 100%;">
134:     <div class="b3-list b3-list--border b3-list--background" style="max-height: 400px; overflow-y: auto;">
135:         {#if loading}
136:             <div class="b3-list-item" style="color: var(--b3-theme-on-surface); padding: 16px; text-align: center;">
137:                 {i18n.loading ?? "加载中…"}
138:             </div>
139:         {:else if roots.length === 0}
140:             <div class="b3-list-item" style="color: var(--b3-theme-on-surface); padding: 16px; text-align: center;">
141:                 {i18n.noFolderSelected ?? "尚未选择任何文件夹"}
142:             </div>
143:         {:else}
144:             {#each roots as root (root.path)}
145:                 {@const rTotal = root.imageCount + root.videoCount}
146:                 <div
147:                     class="b3-list-item b3-list-item--narrow toggle"
148:                     class:b3-list-item--focus={selectedDir === root.path}
149:                     style:opacity={rTotal > 0 ? "1" : "0.45"}
150:                     onclick={() => selectDir(root.path, rTotal)}
151:                     onkeydown={undefined}
152:                     role="button"
153:                     tabindex="0"
154:                 >
155:                     {#if root.hasSubdirs}
156:                         <span class="b3-list-item__toggle b3-list-item__toggle--hl"
157:                             onclick={(e: MouseEvent) => { e.stopPropagation(); expandChild(root) }}
158:                             onkeydown={undefined}
159:                             role="button"
160:                             tabindex="0">
161:                             <svg class="b3-list-item__arrow" class:b3-list-item__arrow--open={root.open}>
162:                                 <use xlink:href="#iconRight"></use>
163:                             </svg>
164:                         </span>
165:                     {/if}
166:                     <span class="b3-list-item__text fn__flex-1"
167:                         style:color={isAlreadyAdded(root.path) ? 'var(--b3-theme-primary)' : ''}>
168:                         <svg style="width:14px;height:14px;margin-right:4px;vertical-align:middle">
169:                             <use xlink:href="#iconFolder"></use>
170:                         </svg>
171:                         {root.name}/
172:                         <span style="color: var(--b3-theme-on-surface); font-size: 0.85em; margin-left: 8px;">
173:                             ({rTotal} {i18n.imageCount ?? "图片"}, {root.videoCount} {i18n.videoCount ?? "视频"})
174:                         </span>
175:                     </span>
176:                     {#if isAlreadyAdded(root.path)}
177:                         <span class="b3-list-item__action" style="color: var(--b3-theme-primary)">
178:                             <svg style="width:14px;height:14px"><use xlink:href="#iconSelect"></use></svg>
179:                         </span>
180:                     {/if}
181:                 </div>
182: 
183:                 {#if root.open}
184:                     <div class="b3-list__panel">
185:                         {#each root.children as child (child.path)}
186:                             {@const cTotal = child.imageCount + child.videoCount}
187:                             <div

<content>
1: import { fetchPost } from "siyuan"
2: import { packageName } from "../constants"
3: import { debug, log } from "../utils/logger"
4: import type { AppConfig } from "../types"
5: 
6: const STORAGE_KEY = packageName
7: 
8: const APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS: AppConfig = {
9:     activate: true,
10:     opacity: 0.5,
11:     blur: 5,
12:     positionX: 50,
13:     positionY: 50,
14:     localFolders: [],
15:     assetDirs: [],
16:     changeBgOnStart: true,
17:     autoRefreshTime: 30,
18:     disabledThemes: { dark: [], light: [] },
19:     imageOverrides: {},
20:     currentFile: null,
21:     inDev: false,
22: }
23: 
24: function post<T = any>(url: string, data?: any): Promise<T> {
25:     return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
26:         fetchPost(url, data ?? {}, (response: any) => {
27:             if (response.code === 0) {
28:                 resolve(response.data)
29:             } else {
30:                 reject(new Error(response.msg ?? "fetchPost failed"))
31:             }
32:         })
33:     })
34: }
35: 
36: class ConfigStore {
37:     private cfg: AppConfig = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS }
38:     private dirty = false
39:     private ready = false
40: 
41:     async load(): Promise<void> {
42:         if (this.ready) return
43: 
44:         let stored: any = (window as any).siyuan?.storage?.[STORAGE_KEY]
45: 
46:         if (stored === undefined || stored === null) {
47:             try {
48:                 const all = await post<Record<string, any>>("/api/storage/getLocalStorage")
49:                 stored = all?.[STORAGE_KEY] ?? {}
50:             } catch {
51:                 stored = {}
52:             }
53:         }
54: 
55:         this.cfg = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS, ...stored }
56:         log("[bgCover] config loaded, keys:", Object.keys(this.cfg))
57:         this.ready = true
58:     }
59: 
60:     async save(): Promise<void> {
61:         if (!this.dirty || !this.ready) return
62:         log("[bgCover] config save")
63:         await post("/api/storage/setLocalStorageVal", {
64:             key: STORAGE_KEY,
65:             val: this.cfg,
66:         })
67:         this.dirty = false
68:     }
69: 
70:     get<K extends keyof AppConfig>(key: K): AppConfig[K] {
71:         return this.cfg[key]
72:     }
73: 
74:     set<K extends keyof AppConfig>(key: K, value: AppConfig[K]): void {
75:         this.cfg[key] = value
76:         this.dirty = true
77:     }
78: 
79:     async setAndSave<K extends keyof AppConfig>(key: K, value: AppConfig[K]): Promise<void> {
80:         this.set(key, value)
81:         await this.save()
82:     }
83: 
84:     snapshot(): Readonly<AppConfig> {
85:         return { ...this.cfg }
86:     }
87: 
88:     async reset(): Promise<void> {
89:         console.log("[bgCover] config reset to defaults")
90:         this.cfg = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS }
91:         this.dirty = true
92:         await this.save()
93: 
94:         try {
95:             await post("/api/storage/removeLocalStorageVals", {
96:                 keys: [STORAGE_KEY],
97:             })
98:         } catch { /* ignore */ }
99: 
100:         try {
101:             await post("/api/file/removeFile", {
102:                 path: `/data/storage/petal/${STORAGE_KEY}/configs.json`,
103:             })
104:         } catch { /* ignore */ }
105: 
106:         await this._cleanPublicDir()
107:     }
108: 
109:     async cleanOldConfigIfNeeded(): Promise<void> {
110:         const stored = (window as any).siyuan?.storage?.[STORAGE_KEY]
111:         if (stored?.crtBgObj !== undefined || stored?.bgObjCfg !== undefined) {
112:             console.log("[bgCover] 检测到旧版配置 (siyuan.storage)，自动重置为默认")
113:             await post("/api/storage/removeLocalStorageVals", { keys: [STORAGE_KEY] })
114:             this.cfg = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS }
115:             return
116:         }
117: 
118:         try {
119:             const files = await post<any[]>("/api/file/readDir", {
120:                 path: `/data/storage/petal/${STORAGE_KEY}/`
121:             })
122:             if (Array.isArray(files) && files.length > 0) {
123:                 console.log("[bgCover] 检测到旧版 petal 数据，自动清理")
124:                 await post("/api/file/removeFile", { path: `/data/storage/petal/${STORAGE_KEY}/` })
125:             }
126:         } catch {
127:             debug("[bgCover] cleanOldConfigIfNeeded: petal dir not found")
128:         }
129:     }
130: 
131:     private async _cleanPublicDir(): Promise<void> {
132:         try {
133:             const files = await post<any[]>("/api/file/readDir", {
134:                 path: `/data/public/${STORAGE_KEY}/`,
135:             })
136:             if (!Array.isArray(files)) return
137:             for (const file of files) {
138:                 if (file.isDir) continue
139:                 try {
140:                     await post("/api/file/removeFile", {
141:                         path: `/data/public/${STORAGE_KEY}/${file.name}`,
142:                     })
143:                 } catch { /* ignore */ }
144:             }
145:         } catch { /* ignore */ }
146:     }
147: 
148:     _resetForTest(): void {
149:         this.cfg = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS }
150:         this.dirty = false
151:         this.ready = false
152:     }
153: }
154: 
155: export const configStore = new ConfigStore()

(End of file - total 155 lines)

<content>
1: import {
2:     Plugin,
3:     getFrontend,
4: } from "siyuan"
5: 
6: import { svelteDialog } from "./libs/dialog"
7: import { configStore } from "./stores/config"
8: import { destroyBgLayer, createBgLayer, renderImage, renderVideo, changeOpacity, changeBlur, changePosition, setVisible, startAutoRefresh, stopAutoRefresh } from "./services/bgRender"
9: import { scanAll, pickRandom } from "./services/sourceManager"
10: import { diyIcon, pickDefaultBackground, DEFAULT_BACKGROUNDS, IMAGE_EXTS, VIDEO_EXTS } from "./constants"
11: import { debug, log } from "./utils/logger"
12: import { isCurrentThemeDisabled, watchTheme } from "./utils/theme"
13: import SettingsPanel from "./ui/settings/settings.svelte"
14: import { buildTopBarMenu } from "./ui/topbar-menu"
15: 
16: export { svelteDialog }
17: 
18: export default class BgCoverPlugin extends Plugin {
19: 
20:     public isMobileLayout: boolean
21:     private _unwatchTheme: (() => void) | null = null
22: 
23:     async onload() {
24:         const frontEnd = getFrontend()
25:         this.isMobileLayout = frontEnd === "mobile" || frontEnd === "browser-mobile"
26: 
27:         await configStore.load()
28: 
29:         await configStore.cleanOldConfigIfNeeded()
30: 
31:         ;(window as any).bgCoverPlugin = {

33:             isMobileLayout: this.isMobileLayout,
34:             plugin: this,
