36:         }
37: 
38:         this.addIcons(diyIcon.iconLogo)
39: 
40:         this.addCommand({ langKey: "selectPictureManualLabel", hotkey: "⇧⌘F6", callback: () => this.openSetting("sources") })
41:         this.addCommand({ langKey: "selectPictureRandomLabel", hotkey: "⇧⌘F7", callback: () => this.randomSelect() })
42:         this.addCommand({ langKey: "openBackgroundLabel", hotkey: "⇧⌘F4", callback: () => this.toggleBackground() })
43:         this.addCommand({ langKey: "reduceBackgroundOpacityLabel", hotkey: "⇧⌘7", callback: () => {
44:             const v = Math.max(0, configStore.get("opacity") - 0.05)
45:             configStore.setAndSave("opacity", v)
46:             changeOpacity(v)
47:         }})
48:         this.addCommand({ langKey: "addBackgroundOpacityLabel", hotkey: "⇧⌘8", callback: () => {
49:             const v = Math.min(1, configStore.get("opacity") + 0.05)
50:             configStore.setAndSave("opacity", v)
51:             changeOpacity(v)
52:         }})
53:         this.addCommand({ langKey: "reduceBackgroundBlurLabel", hotkey: "⇧⌘9", callback: () => {
54:             const v = Math.max(0, configStore.get("blur") - 1)
55:             configStore.setAndSave("blur", v)
56:             changeBlur(v)
57:         }})
58:         this.addCommand({ langKey: "addBackgroundBlurLabel", hotkey: "⇧⌘0", callback: () => {
59:             const v = Math.min(10, configStore.get("blur") + 1)
60:             configStore.setAndSave("blur", v)
61:             changeBlur(v)
62:         }})
63: 
64:         if (configStore.get("activate")) {
65:             createBgLayer()
66:             if (configStore.get("changeBgOnStart")) {
67:                 await this.randomSelect()
68:             }
69:             const currentFile = configStore.get("currentFile")
70:             if (DEFAULT_BACKGROUNDS.includes(currentFile ?? '')) {
71:                 configStore.set("currentFile", pickDefaultBackground())
72:                 configStore.save()
73:             }
74:             if (!configStore.get("currentFile")) {
75:                 const assetDirs = configStore.get("assetDirs")
76:                 const localFolders = configStore.get("localFolders")
77:                 const pool = await scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders)
78:                 if (pool.length === 0) {
79:                     configStore.set("currentFile", pickDefaultBackground())
80:                     configStore.save()
81:                 }
82:             }
83:             this.applyBackground()
84:         }
85: 
86:         this._unwatchTheme = watchTheme((mode, name) => {
87:             log("[bgCover] theme changed:", mode, name)
88:             this.applyThemeShield()
89:         })
90: 
91:         log("[bgCover]", this.i18n.helloPlugin)
92:     }
93: 
94:     onLayoutReady() {
95:         const topBarElement = this.addTopBar({
96:             icon: "iconLogo",
97:             title: this.i18n.addTopBarIcon,
98:             position: "right",
99:             callback: () => {
100:                 buildTopBarMenu(topBarElement, this, {
101:                     onOpenSettings: (tab?: string) => this.openSetting(tab),
102:                     toggleBackground: () => this.toggleBackground(),
103:                     randomSelect: () => this.randomSelect(),
104:                 })
105:             },
106:         })
107:     }
108: 
109:     openSetting(activeTab?: string): void {
110:         svelteDialog({
111:             title: "Background Cover",
112:             width: this.isMobileLayout ? "92vw" : "max(520px, 60vw)",
113:             height: "max(520px, 60vh)",
114:             component: SettingsPanel,
115:             props: { activeTab },
116:         })
117:     }
118: 
119:     onunload() {
120:         this._unwatchTheme?.()
121:         destroyBgLayer()
122:         log("[bgCover]", this.i18n.byePlugin)
123:     }
124: 
125:     async toggleBackground() {
126:         const active = !configStore.get("activate")
127:         log("[bgCover] toggleBackground:", active ? "activated" : "deactivated")
128:         configStore.setAndSave("activate", active)
129:         if (active) {
130:             createBgLayer()
131:             this.applyBackground()
132:         } else {
133:             destroyBgLayer()
134:         }
135:     }
136: 
137:     async randomSelect() {
138:         const assetDirs = configStore.get("assetDirs")
139:         const localFolders = configStore.get("localFolders")
140:         const pool = await scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders)
141:         if (pool.length === 0) {
142:             log("[bgCover] randomSelect: pool is empty, nothing to pick")
143:             return
144:         }
145:         const exclude = pool.length > 1 ? configStore.get("currentFile") : null
146:         const item = pickRandom(pool, exclude)
147:         if (!item) return
148:         log("[bgCover] randomSelect: picked", item.name, "from", pool.length, "items")
149:         configStore.set("currentFile", item.url)
150:         configStore.save()
151:         if (item.type === 'image') {
152:             renderImage(item.url)
153:         } else {
154:             renderVideo(item.url)
155:         }
156:         changeOpacity(configStore.get("opacity"))
157:         changeBlur(configStore.get("blur"))
158:         changePosition(configStore.get("positionX"), configStore.get("positionY"))
159:     }
160: 
161:     private applyBackground() {
162:         log("[bgCover] applyBackground: start")
163:         try {
164:             const currentFile = configStore.get("currentFile")
165:             debug("[bgCover] applyBackground: currentFile =", currentFile)
166:             if (!currentFile) {
167:                 debug("[bgCover] applyBackground: currentFile is null, skip render")
168:                 return
169:             }
170: 
171:             const ext = '.' + (currentFile.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
172:             debug("[bgCover] applyBackground: ext =", ext)
173:             if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) {
174:                 debug("[bgCover] applyBackground: -> renderVideo")
175:                 renderVideo(currentFile)
176:             } else if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext)) {
177:                 debug("[bgCover] applyBackground: -> renderImage")
178:                 renderImage(currentFile)
179:             } else {
180:                 console.warn(`[bgCover] applyBackground: unknown extension "${ext}" for ${currentFile}`)
181:                 return
182:             }
183:         } finally {
184:             const opacity = configStore.get("opacity")
185:             const blur = configStore.get("blur")
186:             const px = configStore.get("positionX")
187:             const py = configStore.get("positionY")
188:             debug("[bgCover] applyBackground: changeOpacity =", opacity, "blur =", blur, "pos =", px, py)
189:             changeOpacity(opacity)
190:             changeBlur(blur)
191:             changePosition(px, py)
192:         }
193: 
194:         const interval = configStore.get("autoRefreshTime")
195:         stopAutoRefresh()
196:         if (interval > 0) {
197:             startAutoRefresh(() => this.randomSelect(), interval * 60000)
198:         }
199:     }
200: 
201:     applyThemeShield() {
202:         if (!configStore.get("activate")) return
203:         if (isCurrentThemeDisabled(configStore.get("disabledThemes"))) {
204:             log("[bgCover] applyThemeShield: theme disabled, hiding")
205:             setVisible(false)
206:         } else {
207:             log("[bgCover] applyThemeShield: theme enabled, showing")
208:             createBgLayer()
209:             this.applyBackground()
210:         }
211:     }
212: }

(End of file - total 212 lines)
</content>

4: import type { ImageItem } from '../types'

8: const ENGINE = '[bgCover] sourceManager'
9: 
10: export async function scanAll(
11:     assetDirs: string[] = [],
12:     localFolders: string[] = [],
13: ): Promise<ImageItem[]> {
14:     const results: ImageItem[] = []
15: 
16:     const uploadItems = await scanSource('upload', pluginAssetsDir)
17:     results.push(...uploadItems)
18:     debug(`${ENGINE} scanAll upload: ${uploadItems.length} 个文件`)
19: 
20:     for (const dir of assetDirs) {
21:         if (dir.length === 0) continue
22:         const items = await scanSource('assets', dir)
23:         results.push(...items)
24:         debug(`${ENGINE} scanAll assets[${dir}]: ${items.length} 个文件`)
25:     }
26: 
27:     if (isDesktop()) {
28:         for (const dir of localFolders) {
29:             if (dir.length === 0) continue
30:             const ok = await validatePath(dir)
31:             if (!ok) {
32:                 debug(`${ENGINE} scanAll local[${dir}]: 路径不可访问，跳过`)
33:                 continue
34:             }
35:             const items = await scanSource('local', dir)
36:             results.push(...items)
37:             debug(`${ENGINE} scanAll local[${dir}]: ${items.length} 个文件`)
38:         }
39:     } else {
40:         debug(`${ENGINE} scanAll local: 非桌面端，跳过 ${localFolders.length} 个本地文件夹`)
41:     }
42: 
43:     debug(`${ENGINE} scanAll total: ${results.length} 个文件`)
44:     return results
45: }
46: 
47: export async function scanSource(
48:     type: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets',
49:     path: string,
50: ): Promise<ImageItem[]> {
51:     const filenames = type === 'local'
52:         ? await readLocalDir(path)
53:         : await readDirKernel(path)
54: 
55:     const items: ImageItem[] = []
56:     const skipped: string[] = []
57: 
58:     for (const name of filenames) {
59:         const fileType = classifyFileType(name)
60: 
61:         if (fileType === null) {
62:             skipped.push(name)
63:             continue
64:         }
65: 
66:         const cleanPath = path.endsWith('/') ? path : path + '/'
67:         const apiPath = `${cleanPath}${name}`
68:         const url = getFileUrl(apiPath, type)
69: 
70:         items.push({
71:             name,
72:             url,
73:             apiPath,
74:             type: fileType,
75:             sourceType: type,
76:             sourceLabel: getSourceLabel(type, path),
77:         })
78:     }
79: 
80:     if (skipped.length > 0) {
81:         debug(`${ENGINE} scanSource[${type}] 跳过不可识别的文件: [${skipped.join(', ')}]`)
82:     }
83: 
84:     return items
85: }
86: 
87: export function pickRandom(items: ImageItem[], excludeUrl?: string | null): ImageItem | null {
88:     if (items.length === 0) return null
89: 
90:     if (excludeUrl) {
91:         const filtered = items.filter(item => item.url !== excludeUrl)
92:         if (filtered.length === 0) return null
93:         const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * filtered.length)
94:         return filtered[idx]
95:     }
96: 
97:     const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * items.length)
98:     return items[idx]
99: }
100: 
101: export async function validatePath(path: string): Promise<boolean> {
102:     if (path.length === 0) return false
103: 
104:     if (isDesktop()) {
105:         try {
106:             await (window as any).require('fs/promises').access(path)
107:             return true
108:         } catch {
109:             return false
110:         }
111:     }
112: 
113:     try {
114:         await readDirKernel(path)
115:         return true
116:     } catch {
117:         return false
118:     }
119: }
120: 
121: function getSourceLabel(type: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets', path: string): string {
122:     switch (type) {
123:         case 'upload':
124:             return 'upload'
125:         case 'assets': {
126:             const prefix = 'data/assets/'
127:             return path.startsWith(prefix) ? path.slice(prefix.length) : path
128:         }
129:         case 'local':
130:             return path
131:     }
132: }

1: import { configStore } from "../stores/config"
2: import { debug } from "./logger"
3: 
4: function getFsp(): any {
5:     try {
6:         return (window as any).require?.('fs/promises') ?? null
7:     } catch {
8:         return null
9:     }
10: }
11: 
12: export function isDesktop(): boolean {
13:     return typeof (window as any).require === 'function' && getFsp() !== null
14: }
15: 
16: export function isLocalPath(path: string): boolean {
17:     return configStore.get("localFolders").some(f => path.startsWith(f))
18: }
19: 
20: export async function readLocalDir(path: string): Promise<string[]> {
21:     const fsp = getFsp()
22:     if (!fsp) return []
23: 
24:     try {
25:         const entries = await fsp.readdir(path, { withFileTypes: true })
26:         return entries
27:             .filter((e: any) => e.isFile())
28:             .map((e: any) => e.name)
29:     } catch (err: any) {
30:         debug('[bgCover] fs.ts readLocalDir 失败:', path, err.message)
31:         return []
32:     }
33: }
34: 
35: export function getFileUrl(apiPath: string, sourceType: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets'): string {
36:     if (sourceType === 'local') {
37:         return `file://${apiPath.replace(/\\/g, '/')}`
38:     }
39: 
40:     let rel = apiPath
41:     if (rel.startsWith('/data/')) rel = rel.slice(1)
42:     if (rel.startsWith('data/')) rel = rel.slice(5)
43:     else if (rel.startsWith('/')) rel = rel.slice(1)
44:     return rel
45: }
46: 
47: export async function fileExistsLocal(path: string): Promise<boolean> {
48:     if (!path || !isDesktop()) return false
49:     const fsp = getFsp()
50:     try {
51:         await fsp.access(path)
52:         return true
53:     } catch {
54:         return false
55:     }

152:         const currentFile = configStore.get("currentFile")
153:         const wasCurrentInGroup = g.files.some(f => f.url === currentFile)

168:                 configStore.save()

180:         configStore.set("currentFile", item.url)
181:         configStore.save()

183:             renderImage(item.url)
184:         } else {
185:             renderVideo(item.url)
186:         }

190:         if (item.type !== 'image') return
191:         if (selectedItem?.url === item.url) {
192:             clearPreview()
193:             return
194:         }

197:     }

200:         if (prevUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(prevUrl)
201:         selectedItem = null
202:         previewSrc = null
203:         prevUrl = null
204:     }

206:     function loadPreview(url: string) {
207:         if (prevUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(prevUrl)
208:         prevUrl = null
209:         previewSrc = null
210:         fetch(url)
211:             .then(r => r.blob())
212:             .then(b => {
213:                 if (selectedItem?.url === url) {
214:                     prevUrl = URL.createObjectURL(b)
215:                     previewSrc = prevUrl
216:                 }
217:             })
218:             .catch(() => {})
219:     }
220: 
221:     async function clearCache() {
222:         const group = groups.find(g => g.type === 'upload')
223:         if (!group || group.files.length === 0) return
224:         const imgCount = group.files.filter(f => f.type === 'image').length
225:         const vidCount = group.files.filter(f => f.type === 'video').length
226:         const parts: string[] = []
227:         if (imgCount > 0) parts.push(`${imgCount} ${i18n.imageCount ?? 'images'}`)
228:         if (vidCount > 0) parts.push(`${vidCount} ${i18n.videoCount ?? 'videos'}`)
229:         const confirmed = await new Promise<boolean>(resolve => {
230:             confirmDialog({
231:                 title: i18n.clearCacheTitle ?? "清空插件缓存",
232:                 content: `${i18n.clearCacheConfirm ?? '确认删除所有插件缓存文件？将删除'} ${parts.join('、')}`,
233:                 confirm: () => resolve(true),
234:                 cancel: () => resolve(false),
235:                 width: "360px",
236:             })
237:         })
238:         if (!confirmed) return
239:         log("[bgCover] clearCache:", group.files.length, "files")
240:         const wasCurrentDeleted = group.files.some(f => f.url === configStore.get("currentFile"))
241:         for (const file of group.files) {
242:             await removeFile(file.apiPath)
243:         }
244:         if (wasCurrentDeleted) await reselectBackground()
245:         refreshAll()
246:     }
247: 
248:     function openInFileManager(group: SourceGroup) {
249:         const wsDir = (window as any).siyuan?.config?.system?.workspaceDir ?? ''
250:         let absPath = group.path
251:         if (group.type === 'upload' || group.type === 'assets') {
252:             absPath = wsDir + absPath
253:         }
254:         try {
255:             const shell = (window as any).require?.('electron')?.shell
256:             if (shell) {
257:                 shell.openPath(absPath)
258:             } else {
259:                 const { exec } = (window as any).require?.('child_process') ?? {}
260:                 if (exec) {
261:                     const cmd = process.platform === 'darwin' ? 'open' : process.platform === 'win32' ? 'explorer' : 'xdg-open'
262:                     exec(`${cmd} "${absPath}"`)
263:                 }
264:             }
265:         } catch { /* ignore */ }
266:     }
267: 
268:     async function reselectBackground() {
269:         configStore.set("currentFile", null)
270:         await configStore.save()
271:         await (window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.plugin?.randomSelect?.()
272:         if (!configStore.get("currentFile")) {
273:             configStore.set("currentFile", pickDefaultBackground())
274:             await configStore.save()
275:             ;(window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.plugin?.applyBackground?.()
276:         }
277:     }
278: 
279:     async function deleteFile(file: ImageItem) {
280:         log("[bgCover] deleteFile:", file.name)
281:         const wasCurrent = file.url === configStore.get("currentFile")
282:         await removeFile(file.apiPath)
283:         if (wasCurrent) await reselectBackground()
284:         refreshAll()
285:     }
286: 
287:     function pickMultipleFiles() {
288:         const input = document.createElement('input')
289:         input.type = 'file'
290:         input.multiple = true
291:         input.accept = 'image/*,video/*'
292:         input.style.display = 'none'
293:         document.body.appendChild(input)

295:             const files = input.files
296:             if (!files || files.length === 0) {
297:                 document.body.removeChild(input)
298:                 return
299:             }
300:             for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
301:                 if (classifyFileType(files[i].name)) {
302:                     await apiPutFile(
303:                         `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${files[i].name}`,
304:                         files[i],
305:                     )
306:                 }
307:             }
308:             document.body.removeChild(input)
309:             log("[bgCover] pickMultipleFiles: uploaded", files?.length ?? 0, "files")
310:             refreshAll()
311:         })
312:         input.click()
313:     }
314: 
315:     function pickFolderFiles() {
316:         const input = document.createElement('input')
317:         input.type = 'file'
318:         input.setAttribute('webkitdirectory', '')
319:         input.style.display = 'none'
320:         document.body.appendChild(input)
321:         input.addEventListener('change', async () => {
322:             const files = input.files

324:                 document.body.removeChild(input)

331:                         files[i],
332:                     )
333:                 }
334:             }
335:             document.body.removeChild(input)
336:             log("[bgCover] pickFolderFiles: uploaded", files?.length ?? 0, "files")
337:             refreshAll()
338:         })
339:         input.click()
340:     }

342:     function showAddUrlDialog() {
343:         log("[bgCover] showAddUrlDialog")

345:             title: i18n.addUrlTitle ?? "添加网络背景资源",
346:             component: UrlDialog,
347:             width: "520px",

356:                         } else {

4: interface IResponse {
5:     code: number
6:     msg: string
7:     data: any
8: }
9:

11:     isDir: boolean
12:     name: string
13: }
14: 
15: async function request(url: string, data: any): Promise<any> {
16:     const res: IResponse = await fetchSyncPost(url, data)
17:     return res.code === 0 ? res.data : null
18: }
19: 
20: export async function readDir(path: string): Promise<string[]> {
21:     const data = await request("/api/file/readDir", { path })
22:     if (!Array.isArray(data)) return []
23:     return (data as IDirItem[])
24:         .filter(item => !item.isDir)
25:         .map(item => item.name)
26: }
27: 
28: export async function fileExistsRemote(path: string): Promise<boolean> {
29:     if (!path) return false
30:     const parentPath = path.substring(0, path.lastIndexOf('/'))
31:     const targetName = path.substring(path.lastIndexOf('/') + 1)
32:     const files = await readDir(parentPath)
33:     return files.includes(targetName)
34: }
35: 
36: export async function readDirItems(path: string): Promise<IDirItem[]> {
37:     const data = await request("/api/file/readDir", { path })
38:     if (!Array.isArray(data)) return []
39:     return data as IDirItem[]
40: }
41: 
42: export async function putFile(path: string, file: File | Blob): Promise<boolean> {
43:     const formData = new FormData()
44:     formData.append("path", path)
45:     formData.append("isDir", "false")
46:     formData.append("modTime", Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000).toString())
47:     formData.append("file", file)
48: 
49:     const res: IResponse = await fetchSyncPost("/api/file/putFile", formData)
50:     return res.code === 0
51: }
52: 
53: export async function removeFile(path: string): Promise<boolean> {
54:     const res: IResponse = await fetchSyncPost("/api/file/removeFile", { path })
55:     return res.code === 0
56: }
57: 
58: export async function downloadUrl(url: string, destPath: string): Promise<boolean> {
59:     try {
60:         const response = await fetch(url)
61:         if (!response.ok) return false
62:         const blob = await response.blob()
63:         return await putFile(destPath, blob)
64:     } catch (err: any) {
65:         debug('[bgCover] api.ts downloadUrl 失败:', url, err.message)
66:         return false
67:     }
68: }

3:     import { downloadUrl } from "../utils/api"

9:         onSuccess?: (uploadUrl?: string) => void
10:     }
11: 
12:     let { onSuccess }: Props = $props()
13:

15:     let previewSrc = $state<string | null>(null)
16:     let blobUrl = $state<string | null>(null)
17:     let validExt = $state(false)
18:     let checking = $state(false)
19:     let errorMsg = $state("")
20:     let debounceTimer: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null = null
21: 
22:     const VALID_EXTS = new Set(['.png', '.jpg', '.jpeg', '.gif', '.webp', '.bmp', '.svg', '.avif',
23:         '.mp4', '.webm', '.ogg', '.mov', '.avi', '.mkv'])
24: 
25:     function checkExt(u: string): boolean {
26:         const clean = u.split('?')[0]
27:         const ext = '.' + (clean.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
28:         return VALID_EXTS.has(ext)
29:     }
30: 
31:     async function doCheck(trimmed: string) {
32:         checking = true
33:         errorMsg = ""
34:         validExt = false
35:         previewSrc = null
36: 
37:         if (!checkExt(trimmed)) {
38:             errorMsg = i18n.urlSuffixInvalid ?? "URL 后缀不在支持的图片/视频格式列表中"
39:             checking = false
40:             return
41:         }
42: 
43:         try {
44:             const resp = await fetch(trimmed)
45:             if (!resp.ok) {
46:                 errorMsg = `${i18n.fetchFailed ?? "无法获取资源"} (HTTP ${resp.status})`
47:                 checking = false
48:                 return
49:             }
50:             const contentType = resp.headers.get('content-type') ?? ''
51:             if (contentType.startsWith('image/')) {
52:                 const blob = await resp.blob()
53:                 if (blobUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl)
54:                 blobUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob)
55:                 previewSrc = blobUrl
56:                 validExt = true
57:             } else if (contentType.startsWith('video/')) {
58:                 validExt = true
59:             } else {
60:                 errorMsg = i18n.notImageOrVideo ?? "URL 指向的资源不是图片或视频"
61:             }
62:         } catch {
63:             errorMsg = i18n.networkFailed ?? "网络请求失败，请确认 URL 正确"
64:         }
65:         checking = false
66:     }
67: 
68:     function handleInput() {
69:         const trimmed = url.trim()
70:         if (!trimmed) {
71:             validExt = false
72:             errorMsg = ""
73:             previewSrc = null
74:             return
75:         }
76:         if (debounceTimer) clearTimeout(debounceTimer)
77:         debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => doCheck(trimmed), 500)
78:     }
79: 
80:     async function handleUpload() {
81:         const trimmed = url.trim()
82:         if (!trimmed || !validExt) return
83: 
84:         const fileName = trimmed.split('/').pop()?.split('?')[0] ?? 'download'
85:         const destPath = `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${fileName}`
86: 
87:         const ok = await downloadUrl(trimmed, destPath)
88:         if (ok) {
89:             const renderingUrl = getFileUrl(`/data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${fileName}`, 'upload')
90:             onSuccess?.(renderingUrl)
91:         }
92:     }
93: 
94:     function getFileName(): string {
95:         return url.trim().split('/').pop()?.split('?')[0] ?? ''
96:     }
97: 
98:     onDestroy(() => {
99:         if (blobUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl)
100:     })
101: </script>

106:             placeholder="https://example.com/background.jpg"
107:             bind:value={url}
108:             oninput={handleInput}
109:             onkeydown={(e: KeyboardEvent) => e.key === 'Enter' && validExt && handleUpload()}
110:         />

127:         {:else if errorMsg}

129:         {:else}
130:             <span style="color: var(--b3-theme-on-surface);">{i18n.enterUrlHint ?? "粘贴图片/视频 URL 后自动检测"}</span>
131:         {/if}
132:     </div>
133: 
134:     <div class="fn__flex" style="justify-content: flex-end;">
135:         <button class="b3-button b3-button--text"

141: </div>

**6. getFileUrl (fs.ts line 35-45)**

```ts
export function getFileUrl(apiPath: string, sourceType: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets'): string {
    if (sourceType === 'local') {
        return `file://${apiPath.replace(/\\/g, '/')}`
    }

    let rel = apiPath
    if (rel.startsWith('/data/')) rel = rel.slice(1)
    if (rel.startsWith('data/')) rel = rel.slice(5)
    else if (rel.startsWith('/')) rel = rel.slice(1)
    return rel
}
```

For `sourceType === 'assets'`:
- Input: `/data/assets/subfolder/img.jpg`
- Step 1: `startsWith('/data/')` → true → `rel = 'data/assets/subfolder/img.jpg'`
- Step 2: `startsWith('data/')` → true → `rel = 'assets/subfolder/img.jpg'`
- Returns: `assets/subfolder/img.jpg`

So the canvas URL for assets is `assets/subfolder/img.jpg` (no leading slash, no `data/` prefix). This is the correct relative URL that siyuan webview would resolve.

For `sourceType === 'upload'`:
- Input: `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg`
- Step 1: `startsWith('/data/')` → false (starts with `data/`, not `/data/`)
- Step 2: `startsWith('data/')` → true → `rel = 'public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg'`
- Returns: `public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg` (without leading `/`)

Hmm wait, for upload the apiPath comes from `scanSource` in `sourceManager.ts` line 66-68:
```ts
const cleanPath = path.endsWith('/') ? path : path + '/'
const apiPath = `${cleanPath}${name}`
```
For upload, `path` is `pluginAssetsDir` which is `/data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/`, so:
- `apiPath = '/data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg'`
- getFileUrl: starts with `/data/` → `data/public/...` → starts with `data/` → `public/...` → returns `public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg`

But looking at the API rules:
> | `upload` | `url("public/{packageName}/img.jpg")` | 思源 webview 相对路径，全平台 |

So for upload, `public/{packageName}/img.jpg` is correct.

For assets, the API rules say:
> | `assets` | `url("assets/.../img.jpg")` | 思源 webview 相对路径，全平台 |

So `assets/subfolder/img.jpg` is the target format.

- → strips `/data/` → `data/assets/subfolder/img.jpg`
- → strips `data/` → `assets/subfolder/img.jpg`

This produces the correct canvas URL. ✅

- → `startsWith('data/')` → false
- → `startsWith('/')` → false
- → returns `assets/subfolder/img.jpg`

This also produces the correct canvas URL! ✅ So getFileUrl handles this case correctly by returning the path as-is when it's already in `assets/...` format.

## Summary of all paths involved:

### 1. Config Store (`assetDirs` entries)
- Default: `[]`
- Set by: `asset-picker.svelte confirm()` → `assets/subfolder`
- Set by: `topbar-menu.ts showAssetsDirDialog()` → `assets/subfolder`
- Set by: `sources-tab.svelte addAssetFolder()` → `assets/subfolder`
- Normalized in: `sources-tab.svelte refreshAll()` — handles 3 legacy formats → always normalizes to `assets/subfolder`
- Format in config: **`assets/subfolder`** (e.g., `assets/壁纸/风景`)

### 2. Asset Picker (asset-picker.svelte)
- Internal node paths: **`/data/assets/subfolder`** (with leading `/`)
- `getRelPath()` converts `/data/assets/subfolder` → `assets/subfolder` ✅
- `isAlreadyAdded()` checks `assetDirs.includes('assets/subfolder')` — matches config format ✅
- `confirm()` returns `assets/subfolder` ✅

### 3. scanAll in sourceManager.ts
- Receives `assetDirs` like `['assets/subfolder']`
- Passes directly to `scanSource('assets', 'assets/subfolder')` 
- `scanSource` calls `readDirKernel('assets/subfolder')` which calls `readDir('assets/subfolder')`
- The kernel API `/api/file/readDir` with path `assets/subfolder` — ⚠️ UNCERTAIN whether the kernel resolves this correctly (might need `/data/assets/subfolder`)
- `getFileUrl(apiPath='assets/subfolder/img.jpg', 'assets')` → returns `assets/subfolder/img.jpg` ✅

### 4. sources-tab.svelte refreshAll
- Reads `assetDirs` from config (e.g., `['assets/subfolder']`)
- Normalizes with 3-legacy-format handling → `assets/subfolder`
- Constructs API path: `path = '/data/assets/subfolder'`
- Calls `scanSource('assets', '/data/assets/subfolder/')` ✅
- getFileUrl for items: `assets/subfolder/img.jpg` ✅

### 5. openInFileManager
- `group.path = '/data/assets/subfolder'` (from refreshAll line 60)
- `wsDir` typically like `/home/user/Siyuan/` (no trailing /data)
- `absPath = wsDir + group.path` = `"/home/user/Siyuan//data/assets/subfolder"` 
- Double slash might be normalized by OS, but it's pathologically wrong
- The correct path should be `wsDir + 'data/assets/subfolder'` (without leading `/`)

Actually wait, let me reconsider. In siyuan:
- `this.data.ws` is the workspace directory
- Typical: `/home/user/Documents/Siyuan/`
- The `data` subdirectory is at `{ws}/data/`
- So `/data/assets/subfolder` in the webview translates to `{ws}/data/assets/subfolder` on disk

So `wsDir + group.path`:
- If wsDir = `/home/user/Siyuan/` (with trailing /) and group.path = `/data/assets/subfolder`:
  → `/home/user/Siyuan//data/assets/subfolder` — double slash, then path = `/home/user/Siyuan/data/assets/subfolder` after OS normalization. This accidentally works.
  
- If wsDir = `/home/user/Siyuan` (no trailing /) and group.path = `/data/assets/subfolder`:
  → `/home/user/Siyuan/data/assets/subfolder` — correct!

So it depends on siyuan's trailing slash convention. The standard in siyuan doesn't include a trailing slash, so this might actually work correctly. But it's fragile.

Actually, let me re-check. Looking at siyuan docs: `window.siyuan.config.system.workspaceDir` — typically `/home/xxx/Documents/Siyuan` or similar, without trailing slash.

So: `wsDir = '/home/user/Siyuan'` and `group.path = '/data/assets/subfolder'` → `/home/user/Siyuan/data/assets/subfolder` — correct! (Because no trailing slash on wsDir and `/data/assets/...` concatenates to form the correct path.)

Hmm wait, actually `'/home/user/Siyuan' + '/data/assets/subfolder'` = `'/home/user/Siyuan/data/assets/subfolder'` which IS correct if `workspaceDir` is the workspace root (containing `data/`, `conf/`, etc. subdirectories). So this actually works.

OK, so the `openInFileManager` is not broken. Let me not flag it.

```ts
case 'assets': {
    const prefix = 'data/assets/'
    return path.startsWith(prefix) ? path.slice(prefix.length) : path

```
- Called with `path` that could be:

  - `data/assets/subfolder` (legacy) → startsWith('data/assets/') = true → returns `subfolder` ✅

But `sourceLabel` is unused in the UI (only stored on `ImageItem` but never displayed). So this is a dormant bug.

- `data/assets/subfolder/img.jpg` → no /data/ prefix → strips `data/` → `assets/subfolder/img.jpg` ✅
- `assets/subfolder/img.jpg` → no match → returns `assets/subfolder/img.jpg` ✅

All produce the correct canvas URL format.

| `/data/assets/subfolder` | `/data/assets/壁纸/风景` | Kernel API path (absolute, with leading `/data/`) |
| `data/assets/subfolder` | `data/assets/壁纸/风景` | Kernel API path (relative, without leading slash) |
| `assets/subfolder/img.jpg` | Canvas URL | URL relative to webview root for CSS `background-image` |

| **26** | `src/utils/fs.ts` | 35-44 | `getFileUrl(apiPath, 'assets')` | Handles all input formats → `assets/subfolder/img.jpg` | Canvas URL construction | ✅ Robust |
| **27** | `src/utils/api.ts` | 20-26 | `readDir(path)` | Passes `path` as-is to kernel API | No transformation | ✅ Pass-through; correctness depends on caller |
| **28** | `tests/utils/fs.test.ts` | 94-96 | Test: `getFileUrl('data/assets/wallpaper/img.jpg', 'assets')` | `assets/wallpaper/img.jpg` | Tests `data/` prefix stripping | ✅ Correct expected output |
| **29** | `tests/stores/config.test.ts` | 60 | `assetDirs: []` | `assets/subfolder` format | Test default | ✅ |

---

### Issues Found

#### ⚠️ Issue A — `scanAll` passes `assets/subfolder` (relative) to kernel API instead of `/data/assets/subfolder` (absolute)

- **Location**: `src/services/sourceManager.ts` lines 20-22, `src/index.ts` lines 75-77 and 138-140
- **What happens**: `scanAll` reads `assetDirs` entries like `['assets/subfolder']` and passes them directly to `scanSource('assets', 'assets/subfolder')`. This in turn calls `readDirKernel('assets/subfolder')` → `readDir('assets/subfolder')` → `fetchSyncPost('/api/file/readDir', { path: 'assets/subfolder' })`.
- **Contrast**: `sources-tab.svelte` line 60-62 does the same path normalization differently: it converts to `/data/assets/subfolder/` first.
- **Impact**: The siyuan kernel resolves `/api/file/readDir` paths relative to the workspace root. `assets/` under the workspace root resolves to `{workspace}/data/assets/` — this *may* work (siyuan uses a `data` directory). But it depends on kernel behavior and is inconsistent with how the same code path constructs paths in `sources-tab.svelte`.
- **Recommended fix**: Have `scanAll` normalize asset dirs the same way — prepend `/data/`:
  ```ts
  // In scanAll, before scanSource call:
  const normalized = dir.startsWith('/data/') ? dir : `/data/${dir}`
  const items = await scanSource('assets', normalized)
  ```

#### ⚠️ Issue B — Two different normalization logics exist (duplicated, slightly different)

- **Location 1**: `src/ui/sources/asset-picker.svelte` lines 115-118 (`getRelPath`)
- **Location 2**: `src/ui/settings/sources-tab.svelte` lines 57-59 (inline normalization)
- **Location 3**: `src/services/sourceManager.ts` line 126 (`getSourceLabel` — checks only `data/assets/` without leading `/`)
- **What happens**: The same "strip data prefix, return assets-prefixed path" logic is duplicated in 3 places with inconsistent approaches. `getRelPath` handles both `/data/assets/` and `data/assets/`; `sources-tab` normalization handles those plus already-canonical; `getSourceLabel` only handles `data/assets/`.
- **Impact**: Maintenance burden; any format change requires updating multiple sites. `getSourceLabel` is broken for `/data/assets/` inputs.
- **Recommended fix**: Extract a single utility function:
  ```ts
  // src/utils/path.ts
  export function toAssetRelPath(path: string): string {
      if (path.startsWith('/data/assets/')) return 'assets/' + path.slice('/data/assets/'.length)
      if (path.startsWith('data/assets/'))  return 'assets/' + path.slice('data/assets/'.length)
      return path  // already canonical
  }
  ```
  Use this in `getRelPath`, `sources-tab` normalization, and `getSourceLabel`.

#### ⚠️ Issue C — `getSourceLabel` checks wrong prefix (dormant bug)

- **Location**: `src/services/sourceManager.ts` lines 125-128
- **What happens**:
  ```ts
  const prefix = 'data/assets/'
  return path.startsWith(prefix) ? path.slice(prefix.length) : path
  ```
  When `scanSource` is called from `sources-tab.svelte` with path `/data/assets/subfolder/`, it does NOT match because the string starts with `/`, not `d`. Returns `/data/assets/subfolder/` as the label instead of `subfolder`.
- **Impact**: **Dormant** — `sourceLabel` on `ImageItem` is never read by any UI component (only `types.ts` declares it, `sourceManager.ts` writes it, but nothing reads it). However, if any future code consumes `sourceLabel`, it would get wrong values.
- **Recommended fix**: Use the shared `toAssetRelPath` utility proposed in Issue B, then strip `assets/` for the label.

---

### Summary

| Aspect | Status |
|--------|--------|
| Config store canonical format | `assets/subfolder` — **correct and consistently used** |
| asset-picker path construction | Internal `/data/assets/...` → canonical `assets/...` on output — **correct** |
| sources-tab normalization | 3-format normalization → canonical — **correct, backward-compatible** |
| `scanAll` in sourceManager | Passes raw `assets/subfolder` to kernel API instead of `/data/assets/subfolder` — **inconsistent but likely works by accident** |
| `getFileUrl` for assets canvas URL | Handles all path formats robustly → `assets/.../img.jpg` — **correct** |
| `openInFileManager` | Correct when `wsDir` has no trailing slash — **works** |
| `getSourceLabel` | Only handles `data/assets/` prefix (no `/data/`) — **dormant bug** |
| Path normalization duplication | Same logic in 3 places — **maintenance risk** |
| `sourceLabel` field | Set but never read in UI — **dead code** |

**Bottom line**: The system works correctly in practice because the stored canonical format (`assets/subfolder`) flows through all the code paths that matter, and `getFileUrl` handles all input variations. The main risks are (A) `scanAll` not normalizing before the kernel API call (fragile, relies on kernel's path resolution behavior), and (B) duplicated normalization logic that could drift. **No critical path is broken.** Nya~♡

*[step-finish part]*

1: <script lang="ts">
2:     import { onMount } from "svelte"
3:     import { configStore } from "../../stores/config"
4:     import { getInstalledThemes, getCurrentThemeInfo } from "../../utils/theme"
5:     import type { ThemeInfo } from "../../utils/theme"
6: 
7:     const i18n = (window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.i18n ?? {}
8: 
9:     let disabledThemes = $state(configStore.get("disabledThemes"))
10:     let lightItems = $state<ThemeInfo[]>([])
11:     let darkItems = $state<ThemeInfo[]>([])
12:     let currentMode = $state(0)
13:     let currentThemeName = $state('')
14: 
15:     onMount(() => {
16:         const [light, dark] = getInstalledThemes()
17:         lightItems = light
18:         darkItems = dark
19:         const [mode, name] = getCurrentThemeInfo()
20:         currentMode = mode
21:         currentThemeName = name
22:     })
23: 
24:     $effect(() => {
25:         disabledThemes = configStore.get("disabledThemes")
26:     })
27: 
28:     function toggleTheme(mode: 'light' | 'dark', name: string) {
29:         const dt = configStore.get("disabledThemes")
30:         const key = mode === 'light' ? 'light' : 'dark'
31:         const list = [...dt[key]]
32:         const idx = list.indexOf(name)
33:         if (idx >= 0) list.splice(idx, 1)
34:         else list.push(name)
35:         configStore.setAndSave("disabledThemes", { ...dt, [key]: list })
36:         ;(window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.plugin?.applyThemeShield?.()
37:     }
38: </script>

9:

12:             confirmDialog({
13:                 title: i18n.resetAllBtn ?? "重置所有设置",
14:                 content: i18n.resetAllConfirm ?? "确认重置所有设置？这将清除所有配置和缓存图片。",

17:                 width: "420px",
18:             })

20:         if (!confirmed) return

22:         window.location.reload()
23:     }
24:

26:     const backEnd = getBackend()
27:     const isMobileLayout = (window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.isMobileLayout ?? false

<content>
1: <script lang="ts">
2:     import { onDestroy } from "svelte"
3:     import { downloadUrl } from "../utils/api"
4:     import { getFileUrl } from "../utils/fs"
5: 
6:     const i18n = (window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.i18n ?? {}
7: 
8:     interface Props {
9:         onSuccess?: (uploadUrl?: string) => void
10:     }
11: 
12:     let { onSuccess }: Props = $props()
13: 
14:     let url = $state("")
15:     let previewSrc = $state<string | null>(null)
16:     let blobUrl = $state<string | null>(null)
17:     let validExt = $state(false)
18:     let checking = $state(false)
19:     let errorMsg = $state("")
20:     let debounceTimer: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null = null
21: 
22:     const VALID_EXTS = new Set(['.png', '.jpg', '.jpeg', '.gif', '.webp', '.bmp', '.svg', '.avif',
23:         '.mp4', '.webm', '.ogg', '.mov', '.avi', '.mkv'])
24: 
25:     function checkExt(u: string): boolean {
26:         const clean = u.split('?')[0]
27:         const ext = '.' + (clean.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
28:         return VALID_EXTS.has(ext)
29:     }
30: 
31:     async function doCheck(trimmed: string) {
32:         checking = true
33:         errorMsg = ""
34:         validExt = false
35:         previewSrc = null
36: 
37:         if (!checkExt(trimmed)) {
38:             errorMsg = i18n.urlSuffixInvalid ?? "URL 后缀不在支持的图片/视频格式列表中"
39:             checking = false
40:             return
41:         }
42: 
43:         try {
44:             const resp = await fetch(trimmed)
45:             if (!resp.ok) {
46:                 errorMsg = `${i18n.fetchFailed ?? "无法获取资源"} (HTTP ${resp.status})`
47:                 checking = false
48:                 return
49:             }
50:             const contentType = resp.headers.get('content-type') ?? ''
51:             if (contentType.startsWith('image/')) {
52:                 const blob = await resp.blob()
53:                 if (blobUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl)
54:                 blobUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob)
55:                 previewSrc = blobUrl
56:                 validExt = true
57:             } else if (contentType.startsWith('video/')) {
58:                 validExt = true
59:             } else {
60:                 errorMsg = i18n.notImageOrVideo ?? "URL 指向的资源不是图片或视频"
61:             }
62:         } catch {
63:             errorMsg = i18n.networkFailed ?? "网络请求失败，请确认 URL 正确"
64:         }
65:         checking = false
66:     }
67: 
68:     function handleInput() {
69:         const trimmed = url.trim()
70:         if (!trimmed) {
71:             validExt = false
72:             errorMsg = ""
73:             previewSrc = null
74:             return
75:         }
76:         if (debounceTimer) clearTimeout(debounceTimer)
77:         debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => doCheck(trimmed), 500)
78:     }
79: 
80:     async function handleUpload() {
81:         const trimmed = url.trim()
82:         if (!trimmed || !validExt) return
83: 
84:         const fileName = trimmed.split('/').pop()?.split('?')[0] ?? 'download'
85:         const destPath = `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${fileName}`
86: 
87:         const ok = await downloadUrl(trimmed, destPath)
88:         if (ok) {
89:             const renderingUrl = getFileUrl(`/data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${fileName}`, 'upload')
90:             onSuccess?.(renderingUrl)
91:         }
92:     }
93: 
94:     function getFileName(): string {
95:         return url.trim().split('/').pop()?.split('?')[0] ?? ''
96:     }
97: 
98:     onDestroy(() => {
99:         if (blobUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl)
100:     })
101: </script>
102: 
103: <div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 12px; padding: 8px; width: 100%;">
104:     <div>
105:         <input class="b3-text-field fn__block" type="text" style="width: 100%;"
106:             placeholder="https://example.com/background.jpg"
107:             bind:value={url}
108:             oninput={handleInput}
109:             onkeydown={(e: KeyboardEvent) => e.key === 'Enter' && validExt && handleUpload()}
110:         />
111:     </div>
112: 
113:     <div style="min-height: 160px; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center;
114:         border: 1px dashed var(--b3-border-color); border-radius: 6px;
115:         background: var(--b3-theme-surface);">
116:         {#if checking}
117:             <span style="color: var(--b3-theme-on-surface);">{i18n.detecting ?? "正在检测…"}</span>
118:         {:else if previewSrc}
119:             <img src={previewSrc} alt="preview"
120:                 style="max-width: 100%; max-height: 300px; object-fit: contain; border-radius: 4px;" />
121:         {:else if validExt}
122:             <div style="text-align: center; color: var(--b3-theme-on-surface);">
123:                 <div style="font-size: 2em;">🎬</div>
124:                 <div>{getFileName()}</div>
125:                 <div style="font-size: 0.85em; margin-top: 4px;">{i18n.videoNoPreview ?? "视频文件 — 不支持预览"}</div>
126:             </div>
127:         {:else if errorMsg}
128:             <span style="color: var(--b3-theme-error); text-align: center; padding: 12px;">{errorMsg}</span>
129:         {:else}
130:             <span style="color: var(--b3-theme-on-surface);">{i18n.enterUrlHint ?? "粘贴图片/视频 URL 后自动检测"}</span>
131:         {/if}
132:     </div>
133: 
134:     <div class="fn__flex" style="justify-content: flex-end;">
135:         <button class="b3-button b3-button--text"

138:             {i18n.upload ?? "上传"}

1: <script lang="ts">
2:     import { classifyFileType } from "../types"

17:     let errorMsg = $state("")

19: 
20:     async function doCheck(p: string) {
21:         if (!p) {
22:             validDir = false
23:             errorMsg = ""
24:             imgCount = 0
25:             vidCount = 0
26:             return
27:         }
28:         checking = true
29:         errorMsg = ""
30:         validDir = false
31:         imgCount = 0
32:         vidCount = 0
33: 
34:         const fsp = (window as any).require?.('fs/promises')
35:         if (!fsp) {
36:             errorMsg = i18n.notDesktop ?? "当前非桌面端，不支持本地目录"
37:             checking = false
38:             return
39:         }
40: 
41:         try {
42:             await fsp.access(p)
43:         } catch {
44:             errorMsg = i18n.pathNotExist ?? "路径不存在或无法访问"
45:             checking = false
46:             return
47:         }
48: 
49:         try {
50:             const entries = await fsp.readdir(p, { withFileTypes: true })
51:             for (const e of entries) {
52:                 if (!e.isFile()) continue
53:                 const t = classifyFileType(e.name)
54:                 if (t === 'image') imgCount++
55:                 else if (t === 'video') vidCount++
56:             }
57:             if (imgCount + vidCount === 0) {
58:                 errorMsg = i18n.noValidFiles ?? "该目录下未发现支持的图片/视频文件"
59:             } else {
60:                 validDir = true
61:             }
62:         } catch (e: any) {

64:         }
65:         checking = false
66:     }

48:         input.type = 'file'
49:         input.multiple = true
50:         input.accept = 'image/*,video/*'
51:         input.style.display = 'none'
52:         document.body.appendChild(input)
53:         input.addEventListener('change', async () => {
54:             const files = input.files
55:             if (!files || files.length === 0) {
56:                 document.body.removeChild(input)
57:                 return
58:             }
59: 
60:             let lastUrl = ""
61: 
62:             for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
63:                 const file = files[i]
64:                 try {

66:                     formData.append("path", `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${file.name}`)
67:                     formData.append("isDir", "false")
68:                     formData.append("modTime", Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000).toString())
69:                     formData.append("file", file)
70: 
71:                     await new Promise<void>((resolve) => {
72:                         fetchPost("/api/file/putFile", formData, (res: any) => {
73:                             if (res.code === 0) {
74:                                 lastUrl = getFileUrl(
75:                                     `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${file.name}`,
76:                                     'upload'
77:                                 )
78:                             }
79:                             resolve()
80:                         })
81:                     })
82:                 } catch (e) {
83:                     console.warn('[bgCover] upload failed:', file.name, e)
84:                 }
85:             }
86: 
87:             if (lastUrl) {
88:                 log("[bgCover] menu: pickMultipleFiles done, lastUrl =", lastUrl)
89:                 configStore.set("currentFile", lastUrl)
90:                 configStore.save()
91:                 const { renderImage, renderVideo, changeOpacity, changeBlur } = await import("../services/bgRender")
92:                 if (lastUrl.match(/\.(mp4|webm|ogg|mov|avi|mkv)$/i)) {
93:                     renderVideo(lastUrl)
94:                 } else {
95:                     renderImage(lastUrl)
96:                 }
97:                 changeOpacity(configStore.get("opacity"))
98:                 changeBlur(configStore.get("blur"))
99:             }
100: 
101:             document.body.removeChild(input)
102:             cb.onOpenSettings("sources")
103:         })

160:         input.type = 'file'
161:         input.setAttribute('webkitdirectory', '')
162:         input.style.display = 'none'
163:         document.body.appendChild(input)
164:         input.addEventListener('change', async () => {
165:             const files = input.files

167:                 document.body.removeChild(input)
168:                 return
169:             }
170: 
171:             const validFiles: File[] = []
172:             for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {

174:                     validFiles.push(files[i])
175:                 }
176:             }
177: 
178:             if (validFiles.length === 0) {
179:                 document.body.removeChild(input)
180:                 return
181:             }
182: 
183:             if (validFiles.length >= 30) {
184:                 const confirmed = await new Promise<boolean>((resolve) => {
185:                     confirmDialog({

187:                         content: (i18n.bulkUploadWarning ?? "此次将上传 {count} 张图片/视频，确定全部上传吗？").replace('{count}', String(validFiles.length)),
188:                         confirm: () => resolve(true),
189:                         cancel: () => resolve(false),
190:                         width: "420px",
191:                     })
192:                 })
193:                 if (!confirmed) {
194:                     document.body.removeChild(input)
195:                     return
196:                 }
197:             }
198: 
199:             let lastUrl = ""
200: 
201:             for (const file of validFiles) {
202:                 try {
203:                     const ok = await apiPutFile(
204:                         `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${file.name}`,
205:                         file,
206:                     )
207:                     if (ok) {
208:                         lastUrl = getFileUrl(
209:                             `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${file.name}`,
210:                             'upload'
211:                         )
212:                     }
213:                 } catch (e) {
214:                     console.warn('[bgCover] folder upload failed:', file.name, e)

144:         }
145:         const exclude = pool.length > 1 ? configStore.get("currentFile") : null
146:         const item = pickRandom(pool, exclude)
147:         if (!item) return

149:         configStore.set("currentFile", item.url)
150:         configStore.save()

154:             renderVideo(item.url)
155:         }

168:                 return
169:             }
170:

173:             if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) {
174:                 debug("[bgCover] applyBackground: -> renderVideo")
175:                 renderVideo(currentFile)
176:             } else if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext)) {
177:                 debug("[bgCover] applyBackground: -> renderImage")
178:                 renderImage(currentFile)
179:             } else {
180:                 console.warn(`[bgCover] applyBackground: unknown extension "${ext}" for ${currentFile}`)
181:                 return
182:             }
183:         } finally {

185:             const blur = configStore.get("blur")
186:             const px = configStore.get("positionX")

194:         const interval = configStore.get("autoRefreshTime")

150:         log("[bgCover] removeGroup:", g.type, g.configKey)

152:         const wasCurrentInGroup = g.files.some(f => f.url === currentFile)
153:         if (g.type === 'assets') {

157:                 dirs.splice(idx, 1)
158:                 configStore.set("assetDirs", dirs)
159:                 configStore.save()
160:             }
161:         } else if (g.type === 'local') {
162:             const dirs = [...configStore.get("localFolders")]

165:                 dirs.splice(idx, 1)

182:             renderImage(item.url)
183:         } else {
184:             renderVideo(item.url)
185:         }

188:     function selectPreview(item: ImageItem) {
189:         if (item.type !== 'image') return
190:         if (selectedItem?.url === item.url) {
191:             clearPreview()
192:             return
193:         }
194:         selectedItem = item
195:         loadPreview(item.url)
196:     }
197: 
198:     function clearPreview() {
199:         if (prevUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(prevUrl)
200:         selectedItem = null
201:         previewSrc = null
202:         prevUrl = null
203:     }
204: 
205:     function loadPreview(url: string) {
206:         if (prevUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(prevUrl)
207:         prevUrl = null
208:         previewSrc = null
209:         fetch(url)
210:             .then(r => r.blob())
211:             .then(b => {
212:                 if (selectedItem?.url === url) {
213:                     prevUrl = URL.createObjectURL(b)
214:                     previewSrc = prevUrl
215:                 }
216:             })
217:             .catch(() => {})
218:     }
219: 
220:     async function clearCache() {
221:         const group = groups.find(g => g.type === 'upload')
222:         if (!group || group.files.length === 0) return
223:         const imgCount = group.files.filter(f => f.type === 'image').length
224:         const vidCount = group.files.filter(f => f.type === 'video').length
225:         const parts: string[] = []
226:         if (imgCount > 0) parts.push(`${imgCount} ${i18n.imageCount ?? 'images'}`)
227:         if (vidCount > 0) parts.push(`${vidCount} ${i18n.videoCount ?? 'videos'}`)
228:         const confirmed = await new Promise<boolean>(resolve => {
229:             confirmDialog({
230:                 title: i18n.clearCacheTitle ?? "清空插件缓存",
231:                 content: `${i18n.clearCacheConfirm ?? '确认删除所有插件缓存文件？将删除'} ${parts.join('、')}`,
232:                 confirm: () => resolve(true),
233:                 cancel: () => resolve(false),
234:                 width: "360px",
235:             })
236:         })
237:         if (!confirmed) return
238:         log("[bgCover] clearCache:", group.files.length, "files")
239:         const wasCurrentDeleted = group.files.some(f => f.url === configStore.get("currentFile"))
240:         for (const file of group.files) {
241:             await removeFile(file.apiPath)
242:         }
243:         if (wasCurrentDeleted) await reselectBackground()
244:         refreshAll()
245:     }
246: 
247:     function openInFileManager(group: SourceGroup) {
248:         const wsDir = (window as any).siyuan?.config?.system?.workspaceDir ?? ''
249:         let absPath = group.path
250:         if (group.type === 'upload' || group.type === 'assets') {
251:             absPath = wsDir + absPath
252:         }

255:             if (shell) {

262:                 }
263:             }
264:         } catch { /* ignore */ }
265:     }
266: 
267:     async function reselectBackground() {
268:         configStore.set("currentFile", null)
269:         await configStore.save()
270:         await (window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.plugin?.randomSelect?.()
271:         if (!configStore.get("currentFile")) {
272:             configStore.set("currentFile", pickDefaultBackground())
273:             await configStore.save()
274:             ;(window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.plugin?.applyBackground?.()
275:         }
276:     }
277: 
278:     async function deleteFile(file: ImageItem) {
279:         log("[bgCover] deleteFile:", file.name)
280:         const wasCurrent = file.url === configStore.get("currentFile")
281:         await removeFile(file.apiPath)
282:         if (wasCurrent) await reselectBackground()
283:         refreshAll()
284:     }
285: 
286:     function pickMultipleFiles() {
287:         const input = document.createElement('input')
288:         input.type = 'file'
289:         input.multiple = true
290:         input.accept = 'image/*,video/*'
291:         input.style.display = 'none'
292:         document.body.appendChild(input)
293:         input.addEventListener('change', async () => {
294:             const files = input.files
295:             if (!files || files.length === 0) {
296:                 document.body.removeChild(input)
297:                 return
298:             }
299:             for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
300:                 if (classifyFileType(files[i].name)) {
301:                     await apiPutFile(
302:                         `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${files[i].name}`,
303:                         files[i],
304:                     )
305:                 }
306:             }
307:             document.body.removeChild(input)
308:             log("[bgCover] pickMultipleFiles: uploaded", files?.length ?? 0, "files")
309:             refreshAll()
310:         })
311:         input.click()
312:     }
313: 
314:     function pickFolderFiles() {
315:         const input = document.createElement('input')
316:         input.type = 'file'
317:         input.setAttribute('webkitdirectory', '')
318:         input.style.display = 'none'
319:         document.body.appendChild(input)
320:         input.addEventListener('change', async () => {
321:             const files = input.files
322:             if (!files || files.length === 0) {
323:                 document.body.removeChild(input)
324:                 return
325:             }
326:             for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
327:                 if (classifyFileType(files[i].name)) {
328:                     await apiPutFile(
329:                         `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${files[i].name}`,
330:                         files[i],
331:                     )
332:                 }
333:             }
334:             document.body.removeChild(input)
335:             log("[bgCover] pickFolderFiles: uploaded", files?.length ?? 0, "files")
336:             refreshAll()
337:         })
338:         input.click()
339:     }
340: 
341:     function showAddUrlDialog() {
342:         log("[bgCover] showAddUrlDialog")
343:         const dlg = svelteDialog({
344:             title: i18n.addUrlTitle ?? "添加网络背景资源",
345:             component: UrlDialog,
346:             width: "520px",
347:             height: "auto",
348:             props: {
349:                 onSuccess: (uploadUrl?: string) => {
350:                     if (uploadUrl) {
351:                         configStore.set("currentFile", uploadUrl)
352:                         configStore.save()
353:                         if (uploadUrl.match(/\.(mp4|webm|ogg|mov|avi|mkv)$/i)) {
354:                             renderVideo(uploadUrl)
355:                         } else {
356:                             renderImage(uploadUrl)
357:                         }
358:                         changeOpacity(configStore.get("opacity"))
359:                         changeBlur(configStore.get("blur"))
360:                     }
361:                     refreshAll()
362:                     dlg.close()
363:                 },
364:             },
365:         })

32:     async function scanDir(dirPath: string): Promise<{
33:         imageCount: number; videoCount: number; hasSubdirs: boolean; childDirs: string[]
34:     }> {
35:         let imageCount = 0, videoCount = 0, hasSubdirs = false
36:         const childDirs: string[] = []
37:         const items = await readDirItems(dirPath + '/')
38:         for (const child of items) {
39:             if (child.isDir) {
40:                 hasSubdirs = true
41:                 childDirs.push(child.name)
42:             } else {
43:                 const type = classifyFileType(child.name)
44:                 if (type === 'image') imageCount++
45:                 else if (type === 'video') videoCount++
46:             }
47:         }
48:         return { imageCount, videoCount, hasSubdirs, childDirs }
49:     }
50: 
51:     onMount(async () => {
52:         const items = await readDirItems("/data/assets/")
53:         for (const item of items) {
54:             if (!item.isDir) continue
55:             const nodePath = "/data/assets/" + item.name
56:             const { imageCount, videoCount, hasSubdirs } = await scanDir(nodePath)
57:             roots.push({
58:                 name: item.name,
59:                 path: nodePath,
60:                 imageCount,
61:                 videoCount,
62:                 children: [],
63:                 open: false,
64:                 loaded: false,
65:                 hasSubdirs,
66:             })
67:         }
68:         roots.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name))
69:         loading = false
70:     })
71:

73:         if (node.open) {
74:             node.open = false
75:             return
76:         }
77: 
78:         if (!node.loaded) {
79:             log("[bgCover] assetPicker expand:", node.name)
80:             node.imageCount = 0
81:             node.videoCount = 0
82:             node.children = []
83: 
84:             const items = await readDirItems(node.path + '/')
85:             for (const child of items) {
86:                 if (child.isDir) {
87:                     const childPath = node.path + '/' + child.name
88:                     const { imageCount, videoCount, hasSubdirs } = await scanDir(childPath)
89:                     node.children.push({
90:                         name: child.name,
91:                         path: childPath,
92:                         imageCount,
93:                         videoCount,
94:                         children: [],
95:                         open: false,
96:                         loaded: false,
97:                         hasSubdirs,
98:                     })
99:                 } else {
100:                     const type = classifyFileType(child.name)
101:                     if (type === 'image') node.imageCount++
102:                     else if (type === 'video') node.videoCount++
103:                 }
104:             }
105:             node.children.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name))
106:             node.loaded = true
107:         }
108: 
109:         node.open = true
110:     }
111: 
112:     function selectDir(path: string, total: number) {
113:         if (total > 0) selectedDir = path
114:     }
115: 
116:     function getRelPath(fullPath: string): string {
117:         return toAssetRelPath(fullPath)
118:     }
119: 
120:     function confirm() {
121:         if (!selectedDir) return

123:         log("[bgCover] assetPicker confirm:", rel)

### 1. HARDCODED TEXT WITHOUT i18n LOOKUP (5 items — MUST FIX)

These are Chinese text strings rendered directly in the UI with **no** `i18n.xxx ??` fallback pattern at all:

| # | File | Line | Current Hardcoded Text | Suggested i18n Key |
|---|------|------|------------------------|---------------------|
| 1 | `src/ui/settings/theme-tab.svelte` | **63, 102** | `[当前主题]` | `currentThemeLabel` |
| 2 | `src/ui/local-dir-dialog.svelte` | **95** | `发现 {imgCount} 张图片, {vidCount} 个视频 — ✅` | `dirScanResult` |

| 4 | `src/ui/settings/sources-tab.svelte` | **412** | `( 图片: {imgCount}  视频: {vidCount} )` | `fileCountSummary` (same key, different spacing) |
| 5 | `src/ui/settings/sources-tab.svelte` | **437** | `aria-label="打开文件夹"` | `openFolderLabel` |

**Details:**

* **#1** `[当前主题]` appears twice in `theme-tab.svelte` (lines 63 and 102), once in the light themes card loop and once in the dark themes card loop. It marks the currently active theme. There is no `i18n` lookup at all.

* **#2** In `local-dir-dialog.svelte` line 95, the success message after scanning a directory is completely hardcoded: `发现 {imgCount} 张图片, {vidCount} 个视频 — ✅`. Needs a template-style i18n key similar to `bulkUploadWarning`.

* **#3** `source-list.svelte` line 38: `(图片: {imageCount} 视频: {videoCount})` — inline Chinese text in the source group label.

* **#4** `sources-tab.svelte` line 412: `( 图片: {imgCount}  视频: {vidCount} )` — same pattern but with extra spaces. Items #3 and #4 should share one i18n key (e.g., `fileCountSummary`) with a template like `{img} images, {vid} videos` / `{img} 张图片, {vid} 个视频`.

* **#5** `sources-tab.svelte` line 437: `aria-label="打开文件夹"` — the tooltip text for the "open in file manager" button. This is in the `upload`/`assets`/`local` group rows and has no i18n lookup.

83:                     removable: true,
84:                     files,
85:                     inaccessible: files.length === 0,
86:                     collapsed: false,
87:                     configKey: dir,
88:                 })
89:             }
90:         }
91: 
92:         groups = newGroups
93:     }
94: 
95:     function toggleGroup(i: number) {
96:         groups[i].collapsed = !groups[i].collapsed
97:         groups = groups
98:     }
99: 
100:     function showAssetDirDialog() {
101:         const dlg = svelteDialog({
102:             title: i18n.addAssetsDirTitle ?? "选择 data/assets/ 下的子文件夹作为图片源",
103:             component: AssetPicker,
104:             width: "520px",
105:             height: "auto",
106:             props: {
107:                 onConfirm: (paths: string[]) => {
108:                     for (const dir of paths) addAssetFolder(dir)
109:                     dlg.close()
110:                 },
111:             },
112:         })
113:     }
114: 
115:     function showLocalDirDialog() {
116:         const dlg = svelteDialog({
117:             title: i18n.addLocalDirTitle ?? "添加本地目录",
118:             component: LocalDirDialog,
119:             width: "520px",
120:             height: "auto",
121:             props: {
122:                 onConfirm: (path: string) => {
123:                     addLocalFolder(path)
124:                     dlg.close()
125:                 },
126:             },
127:         })
128:     }
129: 
130:     function addAssetFolder(dir: string) {
131:         if (!dir) return
132:         log("[bgCover] addAssetFolder:", dir)
133:         const dirs = [...configStore.get("assetDirs"), dir]
134:         configStore.set("assetDirs", dirs)
135:         configStore.save()
136:         refreshAll()
137:     }
138: 
139:     function addLocalFolder(path: string) {
140:         if (!path) return
141:         log("[bgCover] addLocalFolder:", path)
142:         const folders = [...configStore.get("localFolders"), path]
143:         configStore.set("localFolders", folders)
144:         configStore.save()
145:         refreshAll()
146:     }
147: 
148:     function removeGroup(i: number) {
149:         const g = groups[i]
150:         log("[bgCover] removeGroup:", g.type, g.configKey)
151:         const currentFile = configStore.get("currentFile")
152:         const wasCurrentInGroup = g.files.some(f => f.url === currentFile)
153:         if (g.type === 'assets') {
154:             const dirs = [...configStore.get("assetDirs")]
155:             const idx = dirs.indexOf(g.configKey)
156:             if (idx >= 0) {
157:                 dirs.splice(idx, 1)
158:                 configStore.set("assetDirs", dirs)
159:                 configStore.save()
160:             }
161:         } else if (g.type === 'local') {
162:             const dirs = [...configStore.get("localFolders")]
163:             const idx = dirs.indexOf(g.configKey)
164:             if (idx >= 0) {
165:                 dirs.splice(idx, 1)
166:                 configStore.set("localFolders", dirs)
167:                 configStore.save()
168:             }
169:         }
170:         clearPreview()
171:         if (wasCurrentInGroup) {
172:             reselectBackground()
173:         }
174:         refreshAll()
175:     }
176: 
177:     function setAsBackground(item: ImageItem) {
178:         log("[bgCover] setAsBackground:", item.name)
179:         configStore.set("currentFile", item.url)
180:         configStore.save()
181:         if (item.type === 'image') {
182:             renderImage(item.url)
183:         } else {
184:             renderVideo(item.url)
185:         }
186:     }
187: 
188:     function selectPreview(item: ImageItem) {
189:         if (item.type !== 'image') return
190:         if (selectedItem?.url === item.url) {
191:             clearPreview()
192:             return
193:         }
194:         selectedItem = item
195:         loadPreview(item.url)
196:     }
197: 
198:     function clearPreview() {
199:         if (prevUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(prevUrl)
200:         selectedItem = null
201:         previewSrc = null
202:         prevUrl = null
203:     }
204: 
205:     function loadPreview(url: string) {
206:         if (prevUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(prevUrl)
207:         prevUrl = null
208:         previewSrc = null
209:         fetch(url)
210:             .then(r => r.blob())
211:             .then(b => {
212:                 if (selectedItem?.url === url) {
213:                     prevUrl = URL.createObjectURL(b)
214:                     previewSrc = prevUrl
215:                 }
216:             })
217:             .catch(() => {})
218:     }
219: 
220:     async function clearCache() {
221:         const group = groups.find(g => g.type === 'upload')
222:         if (!group || group.files.length === 0) return
223:         const imgCount = group.files.filter(f => f.type === 'image').length
224:         const vidCount = group.files.filter(f => f.type === 'video').length
225:         const parts: string[] = []
226:         if (imgCount > 0) parts.push(`${imgCount} ${i18n.imageCount ?? 'images'}`)
227:         if (vidCount > 0) parts.push(`${vidCount} ${i18n.videoCount ?? 'videos'}`)
228:         const confirmed = await new Promise<boolean>(resolve => {
229:             confirmDialog({
230:                 title: i18n.clearCacheTitle ?? "清空插件缓存",
231:                 content: `${i18n.clearCacheConfirm ?? '确认删除所有插件缓存文件？将删除'} ${parts.join('、')}`,
232:                 confirm: () => resolve(true),
233:                 cancel: () => resolve(false),
234:                 width: "360px",
235:             })
236:         })
237:         if (!confirmed) return
238:         log("[bgCover] clearCache:", group.files.length, "files")
239:         const wasCurrentDeleted = group.files.some(f => f.url === configStore.get("currentFile"))
240:         for (const file of group.files) {
241:             await removeFile(file.apiPath)
242:         }
243:         if (wasCurrentDeleted) await reselectBackground()
244:         refreshAll()
245:     }
246: 
247:     function openInFileManager(group: SourceGroup) {
248:         const wsDir = (window as any).siyuan?.config?.system?.workspaceDir ?? ''
249:         let absPath = group.path
250:         if (group.type === 'upload' || group.type === 'assets') {
251:             absPath = wsDir + absPath
252:         }
253:         try {
254:             const shell = (window as any).require?.('electron')?.shell
255:             if (shell) {
256:                 shell.openPath(absPath)
257:             } else {
258:                 const { exec } = (window as any).require?.('child_process') ?? {}
259:                 if (exec) {
260:                     const cmd = process.platform === 'darwin' ? 'open' : process.platform === 'win32' ? 'explorer' : 'xdg-open'
261:                     exec(`${cmd} "${absPath}"`)
262:                 }
263:             }
264:         } catch { /* ignore */ }
265:     }
266: 
267:     async function reselectBackground() {
268:         configStore.set("currentFile", null)
269:         await configStore.save()
270:         await (window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.plugin?.randomSelect?.()
271:         if (!configStore.get("currentFile")) {
272:             configStore.set("currentFile", pickDefaultBackground())
273:             await configStore.save()
274:             ;(window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.plugin?.applyBackground?.()
275:         }
276:     }
277: 
278:     async function deleteFile(file: ImageItem) {
279:         log("[bgCover] deleteFile:", file.name)
280:         const wasCurrent = file.url === configStore.get("currentFile")
281:         await removeFile(file.apiPath)
282:         if (wasCurrent) await reselectBackground()
283:         refreshAll()
284:     }
285: 
286:     function pickMultipleFiles() {
287:         const input = document.createElement('input')
288:         input.type = 'file'
289:         input.multiple = true
290:         input.accept = 'image/*,video/*'
291:         input.style.display = 'none'
292:         document.body.appendChild(input)
293:         input.addEventListener('change', async () => {
294:             const files = input.files
295:             if (!files || files.length === 0) {
296:                 document.body.removeChild(input)
297:                 return
298:             }
299:             for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
300:                 if (classifyFileType(files[i].name)) {
301:                     await apiPutFile(
302:                         `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${files[i].name}`,
303:                         files[i],
304:                     )
305:                 }
306:             }
307:             document.body.removeChild(input)
308:             log("[bgCover] pickMultipleFiles: uploaded", files?.length ?? 0, "files")
309:             refreshAll()
310:         })
311:         input.click()
312:     }
313: 
314:     function pickFolderFiles() {
315:         const input = document.createElement('input')
316:         input.type = 'file'
317:         input.setAttribute('webkitdirectory', '')
318:         input.style.display = 'none'
319:         document.body.appendChild(input)
320:         input.addEventListener('change', async () => {
321:             const files = input.files
322:             if (!files || files.length === 0) {
323:                 document.body.removeChild(input)
324:                 return
325:             }
326:             for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
327:                 if (classifyFileType(files[i].name)) {
328:                     await apiPutFile(
329:                         `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${files[i].name}`,
330:                         files[i],
331:                     )
332:                 }
333:             }
334:             document.body.removeChild(input)
335:             log("[bgCover] pickFolderFiles: uploaded", files?.length ?? 0, "files")
336:             refreshAll()
337:         })
338:         input.click()
339:     }
340: 
341:     function showAddUrlDialog() {
342:         log("[bgCover] showAddUrlDialog")
343:         const dlg = svelteDialog({
344:             title: i18n.addUrlTitle ?? "添加网络背景资源",
345:             component: UrlDialog,
346:             width: "520px",
347:             height: "auto",
348:             props: {
349:                 onSuccess: (uploadUrl?: string) => {
350:                     if (uploadUrl) {
351:                         configStore.set("currentFile", uploadUrl)
352:                         configStore.save()
353:                         if (uploadUrl.match(/\.(mp4|webm|ogg|mov|avi|mkv)$/i)) {
354:                             renderVideo(uploadUrl)
355:                         } else {
356:                             renderImage(uploadUrl)
357:                         }
358:                         changeOpacity(configStore.get("opacity"))
359:                         changeBlur(configStore.get("blur"))
360:                     }
361:                     refreshAll()
362:                     dlg.close()
363:                 },
364:             },
365:         })
366:     }
367: </script>
