<path>/home/hwang/Documents/Github/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/src/ui/local-dir-dialog.svelte</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>
1: <script lang="ts">
2:     import { classifyFileType } from "../types"
3: 
4:     const i18n = (window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.i18n ?? {}
5: 
6:     interface Props {
7:         onConfirm?: (path: string) => void
8:     }
9: 
10:     let { onConfirm }: Props = $props()
11: 
12:     let pathInput = $state("")
13:     let checking = $state(false)
14:     let validDir = $state(false)
15:     let imgCount = $state(0)
16:     let vidCount = $state(0)
17:     let errorMsg = $state("")
18:     let debounceTimer: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null = null
19: 
20:     async function doCheck(p: string) {
21:         if (!p) {
22:             validDir = false
23:             errorMsg = ""
24:             imgCount = 0
25:             vidCount = 0
26:             return
27:         }
28:         checking = true
29:         errorMsg = ""
30:         validDir = false
31:         imgCount = 0
32:         vidCount = 0
33: 
34:         const fsp = (window as any).require?.('fs/promises')
35:         if (!fsp) {
36:             errorMsg = i18n.notDesktop ?? "当前非桌面端，不支持本地目录"
37:             checking = false
38:             return
39:         }
40: 
41:         try {
42:             await fsp.access(p)
43:         } catch {
44:             errorMsg = i18n.pathNotExist ?? "路径不存在或无法访问"
45:             checking = false
46:             return
47:         }
48: 
49:         try {
50:             const entries = await fsp.readdir(p, { withFileTypes: true })
51:             for (const e of entries) {
52:                 if (!e.isFile()) continue
53:                 const t = classifyFileType(e.name)
54:                 if (t === 'image') imgCount++
55:                 else if (t === 'video') vidCount++
56:             }
57:             if (imgCount + vidCount === 0) {
58:                 errorMsg = i18n.noValidFiles ?? "该目录下未发现支持的图片/视频文件"
59:             } else {
60:                 validDir = true
61:             }
62:         } catch (e: any) {
63:             errorMsg = `${i18n.readDirFailed ?? "读取目录失败"}: ${e.message}`
64:         }
65:         checking = false
66:     }
67: 
68:     function handleInput() {
69:         if (debounceTimer) clearTimeout(debounceTimer)
70:         debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => doCheck(pathInput.trim()), 500)
71:     }
72: 
73:     function confirm() {
74:         onConfirm?.(pathInput.trim())
75:     }
76: </script>
77: 
78: <div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 12px; padding: 8px; width: 100%;">
79: 
80:     <input class="b3-text-field fn__block" type="text" style="width: 100%;"
81:         placeholder="/home/user/Pictures/wallpaper"
82:         bind:value={pathInput}
83:         oninput={handleInput}
84:         onkeydown={(e: KeyboardEvent) => e.key === 'Enter' && validDir && confirm()}
85:     />
86: 
87:     <div style="min-height: 60px; display: flex; align-items: center; padding: 8px;
88:         border-radius: 4px; background: var(--b3-theme-surface);">
89:         {#if checking}
90:             <span style="color: var(--b3-theme-on-surface);">{i18n.detecting ?? "正在检测…"}</span>
91:         {:else if validDir}
92:             <span>
93:                 📁 <code class="fn__code">{pathInput.trim()}</code>
94:                 <span style="margin-left: 12px; color: var(--b3-theme-primary);">
95:                     {i18n.dirScanResult.replace('{imgCount}', `${imgCount}`).replace('{vidCount}', `${vidCount}`)}
96:                 </span>
97:             </span>
98:         {:else if errorMsg}
99:             <span style="color: var(--b3-theme-error);">{errorMsg}</span>
100:         {:else}
101:             <span style="color: var(--b3-theme-on-surface);">{i18n.autoDetectHint ?? "输入路径后自动检测"}</span>
102:         {/if}
103:     </div>
104: 
105:     <div class="fn__flex" style="justify-content: flex-end;">
106:         <button class="b3-button b3-button--text"
107:             disabled={!validDir}
108:             onclick={confirm}>
109:             {i18n.add ?? "添加"}
110:         </button>
111:     </div>

35:         let imageCount = 0, videoCount = 0, hasSubdirs = false

37:         const items = await readDirItems(dirPath + '/')

39:             if (child.isDir) {
40:                 hasSubdirs = true

46:             }

53:         for (const item of items) {
54:             if (!item.isDir) continue
55:             const nodePath = "/data/assets/" + item.name
56:             const { imageCount, videoCount, hasSubdirs } = await scanDir(nodePath)
57:             roots.push({
58:                 name: item.name,
59:                 path: nodePath,
60:                 imageCount,
61:                 videoCount,
62:                 children: [],
63:                 open: false,
64:                 loaded: false,
65:                 hasSubdirs,
66:             })

68:         roots.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name))

73:         if (node.open) {
74:             node.open = false
75:             return
76:         }
77:

79:             log("[bgCover] assetPicker expand:", node.name)
80:             node.imageCount = 0
81:             node.videoCount = 0
82:             node.children = []
83: 
84:             const items = await readDirItems(node.path + '/')
85:             for (const child of items) {

88:                     const { imageCount, videoCount, hasSubdirs } = await scanDir(childPath)

96:                         loaded: false,

102:                     else if (type === 'video') node.videoCount++
103:                 }
104:             }

106:             node.loaded = true
107:         }

112:     function selectDir(path: string, total: number) {
113:         if (total > 0) selectedDir = path

<content>
1: <script lang="ts">
2:     import { onDestroy } from "svelte"
3:     import { downloadUrl } from "../utils/api"
4:     import { getFileUrl } from "../utils/fs"
5: 
6:     const i18n = (window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.i18n ?? {}
7: 
8:     interface Props {
9:         onSuccess?: (uploadUrl?: string) => void
10:     }
11: 
12:     let { onSuccess }: Props = $props()
13: 
14:     let url = $state("")
15:     let previewSrc = $state<string | null>(null)
16:     let blobUrl = $state<string | null>(null)
17:     let validExt = $state(false)
18:     let checking = $state(false)
19:     let errorMsg = $state("")
20:     let debounceTimer: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null = null
21: 
22:     const VALID_EXTS = new Set(['.png', '.jpg', '.jpeg', '.gif', '.webp', '.bmp', '.svg', '.avif',
23:         '.mp4', '.webm', '.ogg', '.mov', '.avi', '.mkv'])
24: 
25:     function checkExt(u: string): boolean {
26:         const clean = u.split('?')[0]
27:         const ext = '.' + (clean.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
28:         return VALID_EXTS.has(ext)
29:     }
30: 
31:     async function doCheck(trimmed: string) {
32:         checking = true
33:         errorMsg = ""
34:         validExt = false
35:         previewSrc = null
36: 
37:         if (!checkExt(trimmed)) {
38:             errorMsg = i18n.urlSuffixInvalid ?? "URL 后缀不在支持的图片/视频格式列表中"
39:             checking = false
40:             return
41:         }
42: 
43:         try {
44:             const resp = await fetch(trimmed)
45:             if (!resp.ok) {
46:                 errorMsg = `${i18n.fetchFailed ?? "无法获取资源"} (HTTP ${resp.status})`
47:                 checking = false
48:                 return
49:             }
50:             const contentType = resp.headers.get('content-type') ?? ''
51:             if (contentType.startsWith('image/')) {
52:                 const blob = await resp.blob()
53:                 if (blobUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl)
54:                 blobUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob)
55:                 previewSrc = blobUrl
56:                 validExt = true
57:             } else if (contentType.startsWith('video/')) {
58:                 validExt = true
59:             } else {
60:                 errorMsg = i18n.notImageOrVideo ?? "URL 指向的资源不是图片或视频"
61:             }
62:         } catch {
63:             errorMsg = i18n.networkFailed ?? "网络请求失败，请确认 URL 正确"
64:         }
65:         checking = false
66:     }
67: 
68:     function handleInput() {
69:         const trimmed = url.trim()
70:         if (!trimmed) {
71:             validExt = false
72:             errorMsg = ""
73:             previewSrc = null
74:             return
75:         }
76:         if (debounceTimer) clearTimeout(debounceTimer)
77:         debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => doCheck(trimmed), 500)
78:     }
79: 
80:     async function handleUpload() {
81:         const trimmed = url.trim()
82:         if (!trimmed || !validExt) return
83: 
84:         const fileName = trimmed.split('/').pop()?.split('?')[0] ?? 'download'
85:         const destPath = `data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${fileName}`
86: 
87:         const ok = await downloadUrl(trimmed, destPath)
88:         if (ok) {
89:             const renderingUrl = getFileUrl(`/data/public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/${fileName}`, 'upload')
90:             onSuccess?.(renderingUrl)
91:         }
92:     }
93: 
94:     function getFileName(): string {
95:         return url.trim().split('/').pop()?.split('?')[0] ?? ''
96:     }
97: 
98:     onDestroy(() => {
99:         if (blobUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl)
100:     })
101: </script>
102: 
103: <div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 12px; padding: 8px; width: 100%;">
104:     <div>
105:         <input class="b3-text-field fn__block" type="text" style="width: 100%;"
106:             placeholder="https://example.com/background.jpg"
107:             bind:value={url}
108:             oninput={handleInput}
109:             onkeydown={(e: KeyboardEvent) => e.key === 'Enter' && validExt && handleUpload()}
110:         />
111:     </div>
112: 
113:     <div style="min-height: 160px; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center;
114:         border: 1px dashed var(--b3-border-color); border-radius: 6px;
115:         background: var(--b3-theme-surface);">
116:         {#if checking}
